Accusation against the Director of the Education Bureau, Lu Renshou: Lu Renshou, the Director of the Education Bureau of the County of Wuxi, has been in office for nearly two years and has repeatedly been accused by people to the Provincial Department. The day before yesterday, more than ten principals from private schools, including Lian Jianzhong, Yao Jiong, and Cao Junmu, jointly filed a complaint with the Department of Education against Director Lu, accusing him of instigating staff of the Popular Education Hall to take specimens from the County Education Association's museum without authorization, which amounts to theft. After receiving the complaint, Director Chen not only ordered the County Education Bureau to conduct a thorough investigation with the Education Association and report back for review, but also issued an order yesterday to inform Lian Jianzhong and others.

Record of the Court Interrogation of the Impersonator: Shen Minhua, a detective of the Detective Team of the Public Security Bureau of this county, led detectives the day before yesterday and arrested Xiang Chongkai and six others who impersonated the Director of the Wuxi Municipal Public Security Bureau at the Liangxi Hotel on the street. Letters and other evidence were found. They were immediately sent to the bureau and transferred to the county for verification. It is now learned that the trial was opened by the judge Liang at 4:00 PM yesterday. Xiang Chongkai confessed that he was 24 years old, from Xiaogan, Hubei. He had previously served as an adjutant, platoon leader, and company commander in the military in Hunan, Guangdong, and other places. He said, "Jiang Guogang asked me to come to Wuxi to be the Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. I don't know where the special Municipal Public Security Bureau envelope came from, nor who sent the telegram. I don't know anything. I did not swindle anyone outside. My nephew Xiang Renfa is really distressed, please release him immediately. As for Jiang Guogang, he used to be a division commander and is now awaiting assignment at the Examination Yuan, you can go and interrogate him." Huang Mingjue confessed that he was from Huangpi, Hubei, and used to be a patrolman at the Hongsheng Wharf in Pudong. Six of them came together this time, but he didn't know what they were going to do. Xiang Zhenyi confessed that he came from Shanghai with Xiang Chongkai. Wang Bingxun confessed that he was an inspector at the Taisheng Wharf and did not know Xiang Chongkai. Gao Hanqing and Cheng Shaoqing introduced him. He only knew that Mr. Xiang was here to be the Director of the Public Security Bureau, but he did not take office. Feng Futian confessed that he was from Huangpi and used to work in Pudong. Xiang Renfa confessed that Xiang Chongkai was his uncle. After the interrogation, they were ordered to be detained for investigation and then sentenced after the facts were clarified.

The Twists and Turns of Inspecting Wheat: In order to improve agricultural products, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mines specially established a wheat inspection office in Shanghai and appointed Jin Wensi as the director. At the same time, Gu Leshan was appointed by the office to come to Wuxi to organize a wheat inspection station to be responsible for inspecting wheat. The Wuxi Rice and Bean Trade Association believes that this matter is closely related to the vital interests of the trade and must be carefully considered. Therefore, a general meeting of all members was held at Yu Tang at 3:00 PM yesterday to discuss the measures. More than a hundred executive committee members and representatives of various trades attended. After a collective discussion, it was unanimously agreed that the nature of this county is completely different from that of Shanghai, so there is no need to establish a wheat inspection station. The entire meeting unanimously opposed it and immediately elected Zhao Zixin, Chen Boxian, Feng Yunxiang, Yin Zhujun, Tao Yin fu, Zou Shaoping, Qian Nianxiu, and seven others as representatives. If the inspection station sends someone to come to negotiate, the seven representatives will be responsible for the negotiations, and seven wheat inspection methods will be discussed and presented to the inspection station by the representatives.

Investigating the Rascal's Occupation of Fulin Temple: Jin Rongxuan and other local rascals in Tangnanqiao, Qitu, outside the North Gate of this county, recently had a strange idea and forcibly occupied the Fulin Temple, drove away the monks, robbed the temple's property, and mortgaged the temple's land without authorization. They then recruited a licentious monk named Yu to be the abbot of the temple. Later, the monk had an affair with a nun and was caught in the act and sent to the county jail. Residents of the area, such as Zhang Jinyun, believe that the actions of these rascals, such as Jin Rongxuan, are extremely illegal. Yesterday, Chairman Ye of the Provincial Government instructed County Magistrate Pan of this county to investigate and deal with the matter according to the various allegations in the original petition.

Agricultural Bank Establishes Grain Mortgage Office: The Agricultural Bank of this county received a notice from the head office that it would be renamed the Fourth District Branch of the Jiangsu Provincial Agricultural Bank from the day before yesterday (1st). The manager of the bank, Gu Shuzhi, also decided to establish grain mortgage offices in Dongting, Luoshe, and Huadafangzhuang to facilitate farmers' mortgages due to this year's bumper harvest. He also entrusted local enthusiastic leaders in Houzhai and Lishe to prepare for the establishment of mortgage agency offices. The offices will start accepting mortgages from December 1st. The interest rate is 1.2% per month, plus 0.3% for insurance and storage fees. If the mortgage is not redeemed by the due date, the mortgage office or agency office will sell the grain. Any surplus will be returned to the mortgagor, and any deficiency will be recovered.

Chairman Chiang's Attitude Towards the NTU Crisis 87

The Moral of Study is Decayed, the Principal Should Take Full Responsibility

The Highest Institution of Learning, the Government Cannot Stand By

Especially Should Realize That Harm to Youth Education

Yesterday, a reporter from a certain newspaper visited Chairman Chiang in his hometown of Xikou. During the meeting, they discussed the NTU crisis. Chiang said that the National Taiwan University was lax in its discipline, and that Nationalists, reorganizationists, and communists were mixed up among them. He had heard of this from his own investigations over the past two years, and it was not based on the report of Minister Chiang. Principal Zhang should take full responsibility for the poor academic atmosphere of the university. However, he saw no need to reply to the letter of resignation submitted to him personally. The university president is appointed by the government, so the letter of resignation should be formally submitted to the government with respect to the organizational system. In short, the university is a place to cultivate specialized talents, and students' thinking should be guided properly. As the highest institution of learning in the capital, NTU is of utmost importance, and the government cannot sit idly by and allow its school affairs to be delayed and its academic atmosphere to be rampant, so as not to harm young people. Educators are role models for young people and should especially have a responsible sense of awareness, he said.

Exhaustion of Jiangsu Province's Education Funds 88

Correspondence Between the Education Bureau and the Management Office

Explaining the Reason for Short Payments of Two Months' Expenses

The Jiangsu Education Expense Management Office and the Education Bureau have been exchanging correspondence regarding the issue of accumulated unpaid expenses. The following is a transcription:

Letter from the Education Bureau to the Management Office:

To the Esteemed Office:

According to the report submitted by principals such as Zhang Tong of provincial middle and primary schools, it was noted that after the principals took their oaths on September 22nd, the director convened a discussion meeting where the principals expressed the dire economic situation of their schools and requested relief measures. At the time, they were informed that planning was underway and that practical solutions would be available soon. Subsequently, it was learned that the Finance Committee had also convened a meeting and resolved several important matters. There was hope that the suffering of the schools would soon be alleviated. However, up to now, the regular expenses of the schools are still in arrears for two and a half months, and the outstanding temporary expenses from the previous year have not been paid at all. This situation is no different from before the discussion meeting and the Finance Committee meeting. It is extremely perplexing. Schools that have income from tuition and boarding fees have exhausted these funds after covering expenses for two and a half months. Schools without such income have exhausted their borrowing and credit. Teachers' salaries, student meals, and other unavoidable expenses are causing daily despair, reaching a point of helplessness. Principals are busy all day, but what are they doing? Nothing but borrowing and raising funds to deal with debts. This is far from education and deeply disheartening. In total, regarding the regular and temporary expenses of the schools, there are currently five urgent needs that the Bureau must address and manage. These are presented one by one:

(1) The regular expenses for each month from August of this year onward must not be allowed to remain in arrears for two and a half or three months for long. It should not become customary without efforts to rectify and settle the situation. When will the Management Office be able to restore the previous practice of paying regular expenses monthly? The Bureau should strictly inquire and urge until the goal is achieved.

(2) The Finance Committee resolved that the Management Office should raise 60,000 yuan within three days of the meeting to be distributed to the schools for emergency relief, and borrow 300,000 yuan within ten days to pay off the expenses for August. However, the Office has ignored this resolution, failing to comply. The Bureau should strictly question whether the resolutions of the Finance Committee are considered valid by the Office, whether there is an obligation to comply, and how to ensure that the Office improves its performance. If the Office fails to implement the resolutions of the Finance Committee, the Finance Committee should be convened to discuss and deal with the matter.

(3) The provincial government has allocated the first batch of treasury bonds worth 100,000 yuan for the temporary expenses of the 18th year, which can be used to borrow about 70,000 to 80,000 yuan in cash. The schools are eagerly awaiting these temporary expenses like a long-awaited rain during a drought. The Bureau should allocate and distribute this amount of 70,000 to 80,000 yuan to the schools in advance, issuing a list for the Management Office to follow, so that the schools can repay part of their accumulated debts and supplement their recent economic activities.

(4) The provincial government has also allocated 10,000 yuan to the Management Office for the temporary expenses of the 19th year. The Bureau should expedite the fair allocation of the entire budget and specify the percentage to be distributed in installments, so that the Management Office can follow the plan.

(5) All special project expenses in the new budget for the 19th year have been announced. The schools have complied with various projects, relying on the funding stipulated in the original budget for maintenance. The Bureau must immediately inform the Management Office to implement the payments and avoid further changes to prevent significant difficulties in the schools' operations.

The above five points represent the universal economic needs of the schools and their common hopes for the Bureau. The unique situations of individual schools are not included in this list. If these five points can be realized, the maintenance of the schools will not be a problem. However, if the Bureau is unable to address the Management Office's sluggishness or if the approved budget is changed or shelved, the principals will be at their wit's end and unable to cope. In due course, the schools will be like dried fish in a fish market. This is hereby reported, hoping for your review and instructions.

Accordingly, it has been found that the expenses of the provincial schools have been in arrears for several months, and the temporary expenses for the 18th year are still awaiting allocation. The difficulties mentioned are indeed real. Prompt allocation is necessary to provide relief. In addition to issuing instructions, Xue Qin is hereby appointed to discuss the matter in person. It is hoped that you will promptly arrange a meeting.

Letter from the Management Office in Reply to the Education Bureau:

Regarding your esteemed letter, it states that according to the reports of various schools, there are arrears in regular and temporary expenses, and therefore, please urgently find ways to provide relief and appoint personnel for face-to-face discussions and promptly arrange a meeting. Upon review, the five points mentioned in the report by principals such as Zhang Tong of provincial middle and primary schools contain harsh wording regarding our inability to pay regular and temporary expenses monthly, implying that we are deliberately withholding funds. This is extremely alarming. However, the exhaustion of funds and the difficulties in handling affairs must be clearly explained.

In the past, the expenses of the schools were paid monthly without arrears. This was due to prosperous years with smooth tax collection and a relatively balanced budget, allowing for ample arrangements without any financial strain. However, since last year, natural disasters and banditry have struck, making it impossible to rectify the situation, leading to a sharp decline in tax revenue. The total income for the 18th year was only 3,003,900 yuan, while the expenditures, based on the budget, totaled 3,905,600 yuan for regular and temporary expenses. This resulted in a shortfall of 901,700 yuan. Fortunately, there was a surplus of 356,600 yuan from the 17th year to supplement the funds, still leaving a deficit of 545,100 yuan. This amount was either borrowed from banks or allocated by various counties, and the income from July and August of this year was also used to cover the expenses, finally bringing the expenses of the schools for the 18th year to a conclusion. However, this has already encroached on the income of 545,100 yuan for the 19th year. Therefore, at the beginning of this year, we were in a desperate situation with no way out, and the budget was further increased. It is already difficult to cope with the present, and a major crisis is imminent, with the risk of bankruptcy. We dared not agree with the budget proposal because we anticipated the current difficulties.

We are well aware of the urgent need for funds by the schools. Therefore, we have sent personnel to various counties to borrow funds, barely managing to issue the expenses for July. Currently, all the remaining funds in the treasury have been allocated, and we have arranged for a loan of 32,000 yuan from the Bank of Communications and the Bank of China to issue the first half of the expenses for August. Regarding borrowing from banks, we previously invited managers from various banks to a meeting at the Central Hotel, and the Director of the Bureau was also present, providing guidance. We also sent a letter to the Director of the Bureau requesting assistance, but there were no practical solutions. Therefore, Yong Jian personally went to Shanghai twice to negotiate with the banks, and there is some hope that about 100,000 yuan can be borrowed, although it is difficult to reach the target of 200,000 yuan. Once the loan is secured, we will manage to issue the second half of the expenses for August.

We have asked ourselves whether we have spared no effort in raising funds for the expenses of the schools. However, the principals accuse us of ignoring the resolutions and request strict questioning. Furthermore, they state that if we fail to implement the resolutions, we should be dealt with. They do not understand the difficulties of the authorities and do not ask about the difficulties of raising funds, making arbitrary criticisms. Why is there so little understanding? The intention is probably to suspect that we have funds but refuse to release them, accusing us of sluggishness. We welcome an audit by an accountant. The Republican government places great importance on integrity, and all institutions, large and small, should have transparent finances. However, this has not yet been implemented. We are willing to be the first to set an example. Our various account books and receipts are complete. We request that the Bureau promptly send an accountant to audit the accounts to determine whether the income and expenditures are accurate and whether there are any remaining funds. This can be announced not only to the education sector of Jiangsu Province but also to the education sector of the entire country. The budget lists administrative income, but the schools have not yet reported it. We can deduct this amount from the expenses to be issued. We also request that the Bureau send an accountant to audit this as well, so that the financial transparency of Jiangsu's education can set a precedent for the entire country. This is our sincere intention.

In conclusion, all the special education funds received by our office are used for education expenses. Unlike other financial institutions, we do not divert funds for other needs. The methods for raising funds are limited. If we had funds, why would we delay payment? If we do not have funds, it is not easy to find a solution. We dare to lay our hearts bare, hoping for understanding.

Zhenru Defeats Lehua Again with a Score of Three to Zero 94

First Half Two to Zero, Second Half One to Zero in the Scocata Cup Preliminary

The Zhenru football team defeated the Lehua team by a score of three to zero in the Scocata Cup preliminary match yesterday at the Yiyuan football field. Approximately four to five thousand spectators watched the game. Lehua's Li Huitang was reassigned to center back and performed excellently, coordinating well both inside and outside. However, goalkeeper Qu Hongde showed some lapses. The forward line differed slightly from what was reported in yesterday's newspaper, as Yang Renwei and Yang Xingyan were unable to attend and were replaced by substitutes, which did not strengthen the line. Lu Zhongen's center forward position was weak. Zhenru continued to fight hard, winning two goals in the first half and only one goal in the second half despite many opportunities. The lineups of the two teams were as follows:

Zhenru 95

Lin Songfa Chen Bingxiang

Feng Yunyou Tong Rongwen

Liang Guanlian Chen Zhenhe Dai Linjing

Jiang Shanjing Chen Jiaqiu

Zhuang Shihong Zhong Lianji

Lehua 96

Jin Fengde Lin Bingwen

Li Ning Xi Qiaosheng

Qu Hongde Li Huitang Lu Zhongen

Zhang Weixin Wang Jihuai

Wu Jianhai Gao Dahan

Referee Jiang Xiangqing, Linesmen Yue Xiurong Huang Wenjian

Lehua Shows Strength 97

Lehua initiated the attack, circling within Zhenru's territory for a long time. Gao Dahan passed the ball to the center, which landed in front of Zhenru's goal. After a long struggle, Li Huitang kicked the ball, but goalkeeper Liang saved it. Zhenru then launched an attack, but retreated halfway, and Lehua attacked again. Lu Zhongen's shot missed the goal.

Zhenru Scores 98

After overcoming difficulties, Zhenru launched an invasion with fierce momentum. Lehua's goal was repeatedly in danger. Goalkeeper Qu repelled the attacks twice. Zhenru refused to be outdone. Zhong Lianji saw a high ball coming from the left and rushed forward to meet it. At the same time, goalkeeper Qu also ran out to grab it, but neither succeeded. Dai Linjing got the ball at the 20-yard mark and kicked it towards the goal. At that time, Qu Hongde had run out and failed to catch up. Li Ning saw that the situation was not good and retreated to defend the goal. Unexpectedly, a ball flew in, and Li dared not use his hands. He kicked it with his foot but missed, and the ball went into the net. Zhenru opened the scoring, less than 20 minutes into the game.

Stalemate 99

Lehua's line was solid internally, but the forwards were scattered. Lin Bingwen's two crosses were effective, but the central road lacked support, resulting in frequent loss of good opportunities. Once, Lu Zhongen lost the ball by touching it with his hand. As for Zhenru, the army's morale was greatly boosted. The connection was good and Bingxiang advanced along the edge on horseback to an unmanned area, as if to conquer. Seeing that the situation was not good, Li Ning quickly caught up, slashing from the side to block him. Bingxiang was helpless. Later, Bingxiang crossed the ball, and Lianji rushed up to meet it with great power, but his foot was too high and he failed to hit it.

Zhenru Scores Again 100

At that time, both sides faced danger in front of their goals. After about 40 minutes, Zhenru's center forward Dai got the ball 12 yards in front of Lehua's goal, dribbled left and right, and fortunately found a way to go. He shot powerfully towards the goal, and the ball went in from the right corner. Goalkeeper Qu managed to touch the ball but failed to hold it firmly. Zhenru won two goals. The first half ended in less than three minutes.

The Battle Resumes 101

Lehua's momentum suddenly increased, and the ball circled in Zhenru's area for a long time. They won two corner kicks in a row, but failed to score. Over time, Lehua fell into danger again. Chen Jiaqiu kicked the corner kick, choosing an excellent angle, and swept to the left along the goalpost, but no one intercepted it. Chen Zhenhe kicked a free kick 30 yards in front of Lehua's goal, shooting towards the goal. Goalkeeper Qu deflected the ball but missed, and it hit the goalpost. Zhenru's Tong Rongwen, who happened to be waiting near the goal, was about to turn around and score, but was penalized for being offside. Lehua was lucky to escape this goal.

Scoring a Hat-Trick 102

Before long, Zhenru's five forwards were like dragons and tigers, echoing each other and making full use of their connection to directly attack Lehua's goal, without obstruction. Because the three generals in the middle were engaged in close combat, Lehua's goalkeeper Qu was isolated and without support. He recklessly rushed forward to block, and Tong Rongwen took the opportunity to shoot a goal, making the score three to zero.

Lehua Defends to the Death 103

After that, Lehua was at the end of its strength, and Zhenru's momentum did not wane. Center forward Dai provided support from the middle, and Chen Bingxiang got his help and advanced to the edge, reaching Lehua's goal. Goalkeeper Qu tried to compete, heading straight for the left corner, leaving the goal empty. Goalkeeper Qu almost forgot his position, and the crowd roared with laughter. Later, Dai Linjing shot twice, and Qu saved the ball both times but lost his grip. Fortunately, no one rushed forward, otherwise it would have been over. At the end of the match, Zhenru won three to zero, and Lehua was eliminated.

Page 10

Shen Bao National Industry and Commerce Conference Special Issue No. 3

Second Day of the Industry and Commerce Conference 115

Yesterday afternoon and evening, group review meetings were held.

This morning, review of the second plenary session in the afternoon.

Proposals such as protecting domestic goods and encouraging basic industries have been reviewed and approved.

On the Necessity for Export Merchants to Voluntarily Organize a China Export Trade Association by Shou Jingwei 116

In recent years, those who discuss China's economic problems have all paid attention to the development of export trade. In the current situation where commercial warfare pervades the globe, all countries are striving to promote their own export trade in order to achieve a trade balance surplus. Such as the post-war tariff system's trend towards protection, the general increase in population tax rates, the utmost promotion of the national goods movement, and the extreme encouragement of export trade, all are widespread phenomena that have occurred in recent years. China, under this trend, especially during the period of expensive gold and cheap silver, to seek relief for the national economy, it is truly not enough to start from encouraging export trade. However, since the opening of trade, China's export trade for several decades has not been optimistic. The long-term trade deficit, the expansion of foreign merchant power, the oppression of the comprador system, the lack of capital of export merchants, and the unsound organization have all manifested the pathological state of China's international trade. From the perspective of the trade deficit, since the Customs records of sixty-six years, there have been no more than six years of trade surplus, while the trade deficit has lasted for sixty years. The total trade surplus is only over 27 million taels (Customs taels), while the total trade deficit has reached over 470 million taels. Comparing the two, the difference is a huge 460 million taels. The trade surplus accounts for only a weak tenth of the trade deficit. This long-term, huge amount of trade deficit is an irreparable loss for China, and it is also one aspect of the unsound state of the national economy. From the perspective of the rise and fall of important export commodities, China's famous silk, tea, egg products, etc., are all declining year by year, and the degree of decline is beyond our expectations. Raw silk has natural advantages and a long history. Although the quantity and value have slightly increased in recent years, the percentage of the total trade has decreased from 32% (1869) to 14% (1928). Comparing with the world's raw silk consumption, the decline in its percentage cannot be measured by miles. The development and competition of the Japanese silk industry in recent years has put great pressure on Chinese merchants. American silk sales have long been filled with Japanese silk. Recently, silk sales have stagnated and silk prices have plummeted. Even the Lyon silk market, which is famous for selling Chinese silk, may hand it over to others. The future of the silk industry is unimaginable. The Chinese tea trade is even more pessimistic. During the Tongzhi and Guangxu years of the Qing Dynasty, Chinese tea was sold almost all over the world. In the early years of Guangxu, the annual export was more than 2 million dan. After the fifteenth year of Guangxu, it gradually declined. In the early years of the Republic of China, there were still 140,000 to 150,000 dan. In the seventh year of the Republic of China, it plummeted to 400,000 dan. In the ninth year, it fell further to 300,000 dan. As for the percentage of the total trade, it fell from 55% (1870) to less than 4% (1928). In recent years, the competition of Indian and Ceylon tea, the stagnation of Russian sales, and the decline in struggle and appeal almost every day are both regrettable and the future situation is precarious. Egg products are exported every year, ranking third or fourth in China's export trade, and are known as silk and tea. The European, American and Japanese sales markets were originally very large. In recent years, they have been affected by the promotion of egg production in various countries and the pressure of increasing tariffs to restrict imports, and they are also decreasing day by day, with no vitality. Other major export commodities such as tung oil, peanuts, and ham are either reducing imports by seeking planting in various countries, or restricting them by various excuses, and they are all declining. This is the actual situation of some important export commodities in China. It can be seen that the symbol of the decline of China's export trade is undeniable. From the perspective of gold and silver imports and exports, imports have been the most in recent years. In the seventeenth year, the net surplus of silver imports was 10.6 million taels, and in the eighteenth year, it was 88 million taels. On the one hand, there is a trade deficit, and at the same time, gold and silver imports and exports are also imports. This is a special phenomenon in China, and it is also one aspect of the unsound national economy. Therefore, from all aspects, the extreme promotion of China's export trade is urgent and cannot be delayed. There are many discussions on the methods of promoting international trade, which can be summarized into two aspects: the government's promotion and the merchant's automatic improvement. Regarding the government's aspects, there are several points:

1. Establishment of the International Trade Bureau. The International Trade Bureau is the main government agency for subsidizing trade development. On the one hand, it investigates the situation of foreign markets and collects trade statistical data. On the other hand, it provides specialized suggestions and strong assistance to export merchants. At the same time, it has the obligation to mediate and promote trade disputes and financial activities. The British Overseas Trade Bureau (founded in 1917, is the central agency for reporting overseas industrial and commercial information), the Market Development Bureau (founded in 1921, is an organization to promote export trade, in addition to the headquarters, there are also local offices, cooperative offices, and overseas commercial officers), and the French Trade Bureau (founded in 1906, specializes in investigating business information) all belong to this system. The characteristics of this kind of organization are: first, it can investigate the situation of foreign markets for the reference of domestic merchants; second, it can help merchants solve various trade problems; third, it can dispatch commercial officers and correspondents in various places.

2. Export credit insurance system. The export credit insurance system is a financial facility to promote trade. The British Overseas Trade Act of 1920 and the new export credit insurance system of 1926 are guaranteed by the government and the guarantee bureau to guarantee the payment credit of the buyer's bill of exchange issued by the exporter, and provide guarantee and financial convenience. The main facility of French export trade is also the export credit insurance system, which was implemented in July 1928. Its purpose is also to help domestic export merchants. Germany also adopts this credit guarantee system for exports to Russia.

3. Export subsidy system. This is one of the most common practices in various countries. When a certain export product reaches a certain weight, it is given a certain amount of funds or a tax refund method to treat domestic merchants favorably, such as the British silk tax refund and car tax refund.

4. Protective tariff system. Export subsidies are a tool for domestic merchants to drive away strong enemies, starting with the encouragement of domestic merchants, while protective tariffs are a direct method of excluding competitors.

5. Promotion of various trade auxiliary organizations. Businesses such as banks, insurance, and transportation are necessary facilities to assist export trade.

6. Various organizations that encourage trade, such as commodity display halls and exhibitions, all belong to this category.

Regarding the automatic improvement of merchants, there are also several disasters:

(1) The soundness of the export merchant organization

(2) The abundance of export merchant capital

(3) The improvement of the quality of export commodities

The above are the strategies for developing trade in both the public and private sectors, which have been effectively implemented in various countries. However, we believe that the fundamental plan lies in the joint organization of export merchants, and this joint organization is what is called an export trade association. The export trade association not only promotes the sound organization, sufficient capital, and improved quality of export merchants, but also includes the investigation of overseas markets and the guidance of export trade. The key points of its organization can be discussed separately as follows:

(1) The export trade association should take export merchants as the main body of the organization. The biggest reason for the failure of China's export trade is the lack of contact organizations. No matter what kind of affairs, they are all governed by their own. Even mutually exclusive. Internally, it is impossible to avoid competition among the same industry, and externally, there is no solidarity to resist foreign insults. As a result, the power of aggression has not yet come, and domestic merchants have long been unable to support this situation. This is not only the case for export merchants, but it is especially important for export business. To seek the position of export commodities in overseas markets, there must be a common and solid organization of domestic export merchants. The composition of this export trade association must take export merchants as the main body.

(2) The export trade association should take promoting direct trade as the biggest goal. Those who talk about China's export trade know that the trade rights of our country have fallen into the hands of foreigners. The so-called international trade is a kind of foreign trade, or a comprador trade. All domestic native products are exported abroad, and are usually handled by foreign firms. Chinese merchants hand over the goods to foreign firms, and they are regarded as having done their best in export trade. Even if the goods are received, whether they are exported or not, they are left to the foreign firms to handle, and they never ask. As a result, trade is completely controlled by foreign firms. Sellers cannot know the situation of foreign markets. In addition to inquiring about and buying news and ordering goods from foreign firms at any time, there is no other way. Silk and tea are the most severely controlled by this kind of control. Although foreign merchants have various privileges to restrict Chinese merchants, Chinese merchants cannot resign from the blame for following the old ways. Several years ago, several merchants established small organizations to directly send goods to the United States for sales. Unfortunately, the organization was too small and the results were minimal. Knowledgeable merchants in China know that this kind of trade is very harmful. In fact, they feel a lack of capital and talent, and the organization is not solid, so they cannot get rid of the scope of trading with foreign firms. Therefore, the establishment of an export trade association should take promoting direct trade as the most important goal, so that the common organization, capital, and courage of export merchants can be strengthened, and specialized talents can also be recruited. It can not only avoid the loss of foreign merchants' oppression, but also strengthen the faith of foreigners. The success of direct trade is by no means difficult. In today's world, countries are trying their best to avoid passive trade and indirect trade, but China's trade is passive and passive, indirect and indirect. Should we not be self-vigilant?

(3) The export trade association should focus on the investigation of overseas markets. The main premise for the development of export trade in European and American countries is the investigation of overseas markets. The demand situation in overseas markets is closely related to commodity exports. Therefore, the main duty of the export trade association is to conduct a thorough investigation of the economic situation, market situation, and special trade issues overseas. The investigation results should be collected and statistically published at any time for the reference of export merchants and domestic industrial and commercial circles. The items that should be carried out are: 1. Investigate the general economic situation; 2. Report the market transactions and demand situation; 3. Collect statistics on production, import and export, harvest, and commodity prices in major markets; 4. Report on changes in tax, new routes, railway transportation rates, telegrams, and postal services; 5. Collect various reports, yearbooks, and trade magazines published by foreign governments.

(4) The export trade association should take improving quality and eliminating malpractices as its responsibility. Poor quality is the most important reason for the failure of international trade. The most criticized aspect of the quality of China's export commodities is the complexity of the quality and the lack of grading. For example, silk and tea have no less than dozens or hundreds of brands, and the regulations for each brand cannot represent a certain quality. There are the same kinds of silk with different brands in two years. This situation is the biggest obstacle to the export of commodities. In addition, sticking to old methods and not knowing how to improve is a shortcoming in quality. In addition, there are malpractices such as adulteration and counterfeiting, such as adding water to cotton. All these malpractices of the export trade association, with the same interests at stake, are very suitable to find ways to improve and eliminate the long-standing malpractices, so as to maintain the credit of commodities in the international market.

(5) The export trade association also pays attention to the research on trade management methods and export technology. Whether trade develops depends on the quality of trade management methods and export technology. China does not pay attention to this kind of management methods and technology, and this is the key to foreign trade. For example, the precise research of export commodities, the procedures for customs declaration and export, the situation of foreign shipping, the methods of foreign insurance, the inspection procedures of export goods, the special habits of overseas markets, the research on overseas sales methods, the contact and remittance methods of overseas financial institutions, etc. are all so-called export technology. This kind of technology cannot be achieved without the precise research of specialized talents. The effect of the research is not limited to one exporter. Therefore, this kind of progress is also what the export trade association must pay attention to.

In short, the organization of export trade associations has long been very effective in European and American countries. Under this kind of trade situation in China, it is a plan that cannot be delayed. It can not only promote the success of direct trade, but also prevent foreign means of consolidation and DumpnigPolicy. For example, the recent reduction in the selling price of Japanese raw silk to seize the American and French markets is a manifestation of the consolidation policy. If Chinese export merchants have a strong and sound organization that can directly sell to foreign countries, then with the natural and artificial beauty of China, why worry about not being able to compete with it? This is why I deeply hope that Chinese export merchants can unite with each other and actively develop abroad.

Record of the First General Assembly 125

At 10:40 AM on the first day, Chairman Kong Xiangxi announced the opening of the meeting. The military band played music. All members stood and sang the party song, performing the ritual. The chairman read the will of the Premier. The entire venue was silent for three minutes. Then, Chairman Kong gave an opening speech, followed by speeches from Sun Ke, representative of the Central Party Headquarters, Wang Chonghui, representative of the National Government, Shao Lizi, representative of Chairman Chiang, and Hu Mai, representative of the Executive Yuan. Finally, guest speakers spoke, and member representatives Yang Xingfo and Liu Mianzhi spoke. The ceremony concluded with music.

Discussion Situation 126

The meeting was held at the Lizhi Society at 3:00 PM on the first day, with 135 people present. Chairman Kong Xiangxi reported on the arrangement of seats, in order of the number of strokes in surnames, and encouraged members to make the implementation of resolutions the top priority, hoping that the results of the Industrial and Commercial Conference would bring practical results to the industrial and commercial sectors. Finally, he stated that the review committees of each group had been determined, and if anyone requested changes, they should notify the secretariat. Regarding the establishment of a chairman group or chairman in each group, please discuss. Member Ding Jingchen proposed that each group should have one chairman, and if the chairman is absent, someone can be appointed as acting chairman. Put to a vote, the majority raised their hands in favor, and it was passed. The chairman also reported that each group would hold a review meeting on the 2nd, and at the general assembly on the 3rd, the members would elect a chairman group to jointly preside over the meeting with the two vice ministers of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. After the report, the meeting adjourned and the review meetings of each group began.

Speech by Hu Mai, Representative of the Executive Yuan 127

Hu Mai, representative of the Executive Yuan, said briefly, "Now, the industry and commerce of various countries in the world are developing rapidly. Looking back at the industry and commerce of our country, we are lagging behind by not a small margin. Moreover, years of internal strife have made everything incomparable to others. Now, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce is convening a National Industrial and Commercial Conference, which coincides with the time of the suppression of the rebellion. It is a good time for our country's industry and commerce to seek development. I sincerely hope that the colleagues of the Industrial and Commercial Conference will express their opinions and deliberate on the general outline of industrial and commercial development in this conference, so that the whole country can follow it for implementation. Hu Mai, on behalf of the Executive Yuan, expresses his infinite congratulations."

Speech by Member Yang Xingfo 128

Yang Xingfo briefly said, "The Industrial and Commercial Conference can be called the Industrial and Commercial Group Conference of the National Conference. The National Government has already held group meetings for education, Mongolian and Tibetan affairs, internal affairs, finance, etc. ㈠ We represent the people and come here, not a joint meeting of various industries. We should not argue based on the interests of various industries. We should start from the perspective of the national economy to solve the current industrial and commercial promotion methods. ㈡ Members cannot be fully satisfied before the meeting, leading to disappointment after the meeting. Some people regard the meeting as omnipotent, and use the meeting to resolve matters that cannot be resolved. In fact, it is not. On the one hand, the government must vigorously implement its resolutions, but members should not expect too much. The realization of the plan cannot be realized by government orders alone. It must be brought to the community and earnestly implemented by all of you present to truly realize the spirit of the meeting."

Speech by Guest Chen Yi 129

Chen Yi said in his speech that he had about two points of thought: ㈠ The timing of the meeting is excellent. Today's meeting coincides with the aftermath of the suppression of the rebellion. ㈡ The development of industry and commerce must rely on psychological stability. In the future, we can use the meaning of stability to achieve the development of economy and industry and commerce.

A Glimpse of the Proposals 141

Proposal from the Shanghai Cosmetics Association

The Shanghai Cosmetics Industry Association, in view of the impact of imported goods on the industry in recent years, and the soaring raw material prices due to the rise in gold prices, and the slump in business, especially proposed to the National Industrial and Commercial Conference, requesting the government to exempt raw material tax and domestic product tax to reduce costs, increase import taxes on finished goods and maintain domestic goods. The original text is as follows: It is for suggestion, I respectfully read Dr. Sun Yat-sen's industrial plan, which says that there are three major wars, one is international war, the second is commercial war, and the third is class war. For us who are in business, commercial war has no ethnic distinction or national boundary limitation. Since the European War, foreign goods have become more and more abundant in our country. The imperialists have changed their military war to commercial war. The people in the market do not understand the advantages and disadvantages, and selling foreign goods is no different from helping the tiger to abuse, causing the domestic production to decline and they then monopolize the market. Their methods are cruel, and the losses to our people are no less than the iron and blood war with strong oppression. Take the cosmetics industry as an example. The import of imported goods has exceeded 4.3 million, and the production of domestic goods is less than one-tenth, the annual outflow of rights and interests is unbearable. Thinking of this, it is really regrettable that the association cannot keep silent. Therefore, there is a proposal to exempt raw material tax and domestic product tax to reduce costs, increase import taxes on finished goods and maintain domestic goods. I have inquired about the raw materials needed by the industry, in addition to domestic ones, such as Essenticloilg pure essential oil and Suthetic Chemical containing fragrance, medicinal compound Oils mixed essential raw materials, there are three types that must rely on foreign countries. It is because our country's civilization has degenerated and science is backward. It is not that the industry enjoys using foreign goods. The import tax on the above three categories is 17.5%, which is 5% higher than the export tax of European and American countries. The authorities regard the import of foreign goods as a good intention to prohibit them, but we must know that our country still lacks the possibility of producing the above three categories of raw materials, and there are no substitutes. In recent years, the rise in gold prices has affected the industry even more. Larger factories can barely maintain, and smaller factories are closed at any time. If we do not remedy this for a long time, we will all perish. At this critical moment, how can we sit and wait for death? Therefore, we request the authorities to exempt all raw material taxes that the industry needs and has to rely on foreign countries. It can be hoped that the cost of domestic production will be lighter and it will be easier to promote. At the same time, we still need to implore the authorities to vigorously maintain and exempt domestic product tax and increase import taxes on finished goods, which is enough to promote and gradually develop. Otherwise, the raw materials are taxed first, and the products are taxed later, and all costs have exceeded those of imported goods. Hoping that it can sell well and compete with foreign goods is like climbing a tree to catch fish. The association believes that cosmetics in European and American countries can be recognized as daily necessities, and domestic cosmetics are in the infancy stage. The exemption of raw material tax and domestic product tax and the increase of import taxes on finished goods are necessary to support them. I dare to state the various sections to save the cosmetics industry, which is the only key to commercial warfare. As far as I can see, I respectfully contribute my opinions. I am waiting for the public decision. Suggested by Shanghai Cosmetics Industry Association, Chairman Ma Sheng, duty committee member Mou Yueqiu, Li Heyun, Zhang Shuliang

Free Talk

Laughing It Off 142

—Hai Ke

Man—My dear, please believe me, I only love you. If my body is not by your side, I will miss you all the time. Those jet-black eyes and cloud-like hair.

Woman—Enough, enough, you are used to saying flattering words, I know you will say the same to other lovers.

Man—I only say these words to you, because my other lover is American, she has blue eyes and blonde hair.

A—You look happy today. Why are you so happy?

B—I dropped a full-page (newspaper size) in the downtown area and couldn't find it after searching everywhere.

A—Then you lost a full-page for nothing. What's there to be happy about?

B—But I couldn't find that full-page, but I found a big silver dollar.

A—I was extremely angry today. I almost burst my stomach with anger.

B—What happened?

A—Old Bing next door is preparing to entertain guests and wants to borrow the carpet in my living room. For the sake of good neighborliness, I generously lent it to him. Who knew that after a while, he brought it back, saying that the pattern was not good and the goods were too old to be laid on the ground and did not match their furniture. He wants me to lend them one hundred yuan to buy a new carpet.

Master (asking his servant)—Ah San, did you see a five-yuan bill on the ground when you swept the floor today?

Servant—Thank you, master. I have already put it away.

Three Oddities in Hangzhou 143

—Yan Ye

Someone came from Hangzhou and said that three odd things have happened in the area recently. Odd things are enough to talk about and help, so I hurriedly recorded them and paid them for this talk.

Sun, a villager near Tianmu Mountain, was casually looking at the riverbank one evening when he saw a turtle coming ashore from the water. Its head resembled that of an eagle. He was surprised and quickly captured it. When he looked at it closely under the light at home, its mouth was sharp and curved downwards, and its eyes were piercing, just like an eagle's head. The shell was as black as lacquer and could reflect light. Other feet, tail, and back patterns were no different from ordinary turtles. Sun regarded it as a treasure and took care of it carefully. The next morning at dawn, there was a crying sound in the room. At first, he was shocked by where the sound came from, and then he realized that the sound came from the turtle. He sneaked over to listen to it, and it was the turtle crowing, which was even more surprising. The news spread far and wide, and everyone came to watch. A certain antique shop owner in Hangzhou recently bought it at a high price and treated it as an antique. People from Hangzhou came to ask for a viewing, and the door was like a market. Everyone sighed that it was a strange thing in the world. I wrote a tortoise essay last month and published it in this talk. All the tortoises mentioned are rare tortoises. Now that I have this tortoise, I feel that what I said before is not strange enough.

In Hangzhou two months ago, a 64-year-old woman married a Yang man who was about 40 years old. For a time, the society laughed. Recently, there has been a strange story of a 60-year-old woman giving birth to a child. The woman lives in a certain town not far from Hangzhou. Her husband is already in his twilight years. The family is wealthy, but the door is weak and thin, and only two old people depend on each other. The couple has been living together for forty years without a single birth of a son or daughter, so the two old people are worried about the fact that there is no child to inherit. Unexpectedly, something very strange happened. Last winter, the woman suddenly became pregnant. This spring, her belly gradually bulged, and the two old people suspected it was a disease. After visiting many doctors, they all said that this pregnancy was gratifying. The two old people were dubious, surprised and happy. From summer to autumn, her belly was like a five-stone gourd. A few days ago, she gave birth. At the first cry, she was a boy. The withered Poplar produced a ladder, and a lineage was passed down. The old woman was so happy that she did not feel the pain after childbirth. The old man was even more excited and smiled. On the third day, he held a grand banquet and held a Tangbing feast. Relatives and friends all marveled at the strange thing and were very happy. The only unhappy person was a certain Jia in the clan who was scheduled to inherit the two old people.

The Zhejiang Antiquities Preservation Association in Hubin collects antiquities, which are all rare treasures. Recently, two plum blossoms have been obtained. They are ancient and elegant. In this autumn, the East Fence is still blooming, but these two plum blossoms are catching up and competing with each other. They wither after the cold, and do not fight with pine and bamboo. They bloom before the end of winter and are like chrysanthemums proudly blooming in autumn. They are strange. The plum blossoms are not very tall, with more than ten colors, ancient and clean, elegant and lovely. The people in Hangzhou all sighed that they were blessed.

German Insect Market 144

— Lü Bing

The system of markets has been passed down from ancient times. It is still prevalent in Europe. The Nottingham goose market and the broom and fur markets in other places are numerous and famous. However, they are not as lively and interesting as the insect market held in Frankfurt, Germany. This city has a regular schedule every year. When the time comes, insect enthusiasts from all over the world come from afar to select and purchase good species, and they do not hesitate to pay even higher prices than usual. The items displayed in the market include butterflies, moths, beetles, flies, grasshoppers, crickets, and other grass insects of all kinds. They are categorized for customers to choose from. However, there are also some peddlers who do not have samples on-site but use a fixed-term delivery method. Their insect sales rely solely on verbal contact. Customers only need to specify the type, and they can make a reservation, just like American itinerant livestock traders whose goods are shipped from thousands of miles away. These people are very familiar with the names of rare insects and where to find them. If there is a demand during the market period and the insect has not yet emerged, they can also issue a guarantee to the buyer and deliver it on schedule. The trade of insects is so prosperous. This is something that those who love novelty should know.

Trivial Talks While Holding Crabs 145

— Wang Meiqu

On Wednesday (October 29th) afternoon, the dark clouds hung heavy and the rain beat fiercely on the tiles. I sat idly in the west chamber, struggling to compose a verse ending with "In the human calamity, the world is turned upside down; in the heavens, the wind still blows off hats." Suddenly, I heard the sound of a bell, and Mr. Xu Jianfu invited me to Qingfeng Mingyue Lodge for a crab-eating and wine-drinking pleasure. I braved the wind and rain and drove there. The wine was strong and the crabs were plump. The trivial talks were all noteworthy, as recorded below.

Rare Coincidence: Jianfu greeted me warmly. Entering the room, we laughed and chatted. I counted on my fingers that Jianfu's and his wife's birthdays were approaching, and I planned a drinking celebration. His wife said, "Birthday feasting is meaningless." Then she pointed to her sister-in-law and her adopted daughter, saying that these two did not know the month and day of their birth. It turned out that Madam Xu was kidnapped by bandits when she was young, and her adopted daughter was an abandoned infant. Her father was a famous scholar who only knew how to mourn his deceased wife and no longer remembered the date of his beloved daughter's birth. I said, "Truly, there is a rare coincidence."

Quick Words from a Quick Mind: Once the crabs were on the plate, some were pointed and some were round. Everyone chose their favorite. Some ate the crab shell first and then held the claws, while others nibbled at the eight legs, saving the crab shell for last. Shen Gongshijia carefully picked and scraped the crab. Madam Xu laughed at him, saying, "If you are so meticulous, why not just swallow it whole for a quick pleasure?" Everyone laughed loudly. Seeing Madam Xu in front of the wine cup, she chewed and spat out the shell and meat of the eight legs and two claws, no less than Wu Yanghou's wild eating style. Such a quick-witted person is bound to have such quick words.

The Reputation of the Altar is High: Zhong Ziji arrived late. He picked up the remaining crab and discarded the crab shell, only eating the legs. It turned out that he had a peculiar fondness for sheep dates. I said, "In such wind and rain, where have you been traveling? Are you going to repeat the mistake of Fangfeng?" Ziji ate and replied, "Your words are about to be announced to you. My teacher, Jianfu, served as an official and educator in Guangdong for many years. After returning to Shanghai, his fame attracted eager students from home and abroad who competed to join his school. Later, he followed the public's opinion and advertised widely in the newspaper, reaching as many as three thousand. In recent years, he has become more selective and no longer accepts students, which makes those who secretly admire him feel disappointed. I, Feng Ruomei, Chen Jianzi, and others, especially feel the transforming power of timely rain and pity those who yearn outside the walls of the school. We ask for the revival of the altar. Today, we are working with fellow students to establish bylaws and discuss organizational laws, which is not comparable to the Fangfeng clan." I noted that Jianfu had many disciples. These few had already entered the hall and ascended the room, making a name for themselves in the art world. Recently, among the female disciples, sisters such as Tuo Fa Hua and Yu Yun, I treat them as respected friends, which shows that the reputation of the altar is high.

Not a Shallow Revival: As the wine waned and people grew drunk, the two Madams served the guests ginger juice mixed with sugar and crushed ice. Jianfu leaned on his wife's shoulder and whispered privately. His wife shook her head repeatedly, smiling but not speaking. I happened to see it, and Jianfu said, "Don't laugh, we old couple are already middle-aged, so it doesn't hurt to flirt in front of guests." I said, "The old man's revival is not shallow. Are you not afraid of the ghost of the gutless fellow?" Just as his wife was about to reply, Ziji suddenly came from the back room and said to me, "My teacher has newly established rules for enrolling students. Please spread the word far and wide that anyone who attaches a one-cent stamp can request detailed information from Qingfeng Mingyue Lodge." After saying this, he left immediately, without hearing our banter. His sincerity was like this.

An Interesting Account of Being Robbed 146

— Zheng Yimei

The night before last, the wind and rain were raging. I was feeling depressed and had no way to relieve myself, so I lay on the couch to rest. Suddenly, two burly men unexpectedly came upstairs and entered my room directly, shouting for the servant to come. I was very surprised. The burly men, seeing me, also loudly ordered me to come downstairs. I couldn't understand why and scolded them. Then several more people came up the stairs, rolling up their sleeves to help the abuse. I realized that they were bandits. My weak strength was no match for their fists, so I could only submit and obey their orders. They drove my wife and me to the side room downstairs. At that time, the men and women living together had already been forced to sit in a row. The bandits stood at the door, holding guns and facing each other, ordering us men to face the wall and not look. The other bandits went upstairs again, overturning chests and boxes, plundering at will. The servant was timid and, seeing the guns, trembled and collapsed on the couch. The bandits mistakenly thought she had something precious hidden and searched repeatedly, obtaining two silver coins and a gold ring on her hand, which they snatched away. What was most interesting was that the bandits demanded gold, silver, and jewelry from the women living together. The women didn't understand their language and, in a panic, took a Western-style tie hanging on the beam and gave it to the bandits. The bandits were furious. A maid wore a gold ring, and the bandits took it away. The maid begged and kowtowed to them countless times. The bandits were unexpectedly moved and returned it. It was truly rare for robbers to have compassion. Then the bandits shouted and left. The residents all suffered losses. I checked briefly and found that, in addition to some scattered ornaments and silver coins, I had lost a large leather suitcase, which contained the servant's clothes. It turned out that the neighbors had been careless a few days ago, so the servant had specially placed the more valuable ornaments in a large leather suitcase to prevent accidents and make it easier to carry. Now it had been looted by the bandits, which was completely unexpected. Other broken books and incomplete drafts were my treasures, but they did not attract the bandits' attention and remained untouched, so my joy and comfort can be imagined. As a beggar of literature, I was honored by the visit of the noble robbers. A smile.

Talking About the Elegant Qin of Bai Xueyangchun 147

— Zhang Mengzhao

I am based in Shanghai, toiling over documents. I have a fondness for drama, but I have no time to study it. Recently, I was impressed by the art of Xue Yanqin, a famous female impersonator on the Tiansheng Stage. I thought of feasting my eyes. So, on the evening of October 25th, I took my relatives to watch. At that time, Yanqin was performing the full version of her signature piece, "Yutang Chun." Yanqin herself played Su San, paired with Mr. Zhao Yu's Wang Gongzi. Their performance was very wonderful. The lingering love in the brothel and temple, and the righteousness in giving money. The most wonderful part was the scene where Su San was deceived and wronged, and the yamen runners escorted her. The allegro performance was vivid and moving, like the cry of a crane in the middle of the night, making people weep. When she was tried in the three halls, a strand of fragrant heart contained resentment and pleaded her case. Her singing was even more outstanding. The audience's spirits were lifted, and the whole audience applauded continuously. Watching the whole play, from the brothel to the grand reunion, there was no flaw. Her great reputation truly lived up to her name. Returning home, I wrote this down.

Acknowledgement and Introduction: Mr. Wang Daren, a famous amateur performer from the sea, has been studying cosmetics for many years. He has a Daren Company in Zhoupu Town. Recently, based on his experience, he invented a kind of "Celebrity Cream." It has a fragrant scent and is as clear as snow. It is wonderful to apply it to the face. Yesterday, I received two bottles as a gift, so I would like to express my gratitude and introduce it to everyone.

Warmth in the Heart (307) 148

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Fifteen: Tears Fall in All Directions, Sorrowful Red Feelings; All Hearts are Captivated, Lingering Green Intentions

Zuo Shichen said, "So you're shedding tears too?" Cuiyun said, "I'm not. I'm lying, my little handkerchief is soaked through three times. First, Lianxiang was my good little sister. I didn't even go to mourn her when she died. Now, the Hong Lianxiang on the stage is the real Hong Lianxiang. Seeing such a gentle and beautiful woman being ruined alive by others, those tears are shed for her. Second, my own life is similar to Lianxiang's. I wanted to die several times. It's hateful that I don't have Lianxiang's determination. Now I think about it, it would be good to die. People would pity her and shed tears of sympathy. We who don't die are truly living a life of torment and suffering." Cuiyun had originally washed her face and was drawing an eyebrow with a pencil in front of the large mirror. Next to her was a large sofa chair. Saying that, it seemed as if she had no strength, so she lay down on the sofa and buried her face in the armrest. Only her shoulders were seen rising and falling, which startled everyone in the room. Zuo Shichen had just washed his hands. Suddenly hearing her stop speaking, he turned around and saw this situation. He said, "Eh? What's wrong?" He quickly came over and turned her shoulder, saying, "It's all my fault. I shouldn't have let you keep talking, keep talking, and reveal your own sadness. Look, your face, which you just washed, is tear-stained again. The others are really waiting anxiously for your turn to sing." He hurriedly called for someone in the room to bring more hot water to wash her face. Cuiyun only sighed a few times and washed her face again. When she left, she repeatedly told Zuo Shichen not to go, but to wait for her to come back. "One or two turns to sing is very quick. I haven't finished telling you about Hong Lianxiang." Zuo Shichen knew that this was a lie. The person was already dead, and the facts were gone. The play was already the aftermath. What else was there to say? However, he felt very uneasy because this conversation had inadvertently revealed her sadness. Fortunately, she didn't have many turns to sing, and she came back in a moment. He could also comfort her. The meaning of life is just like this. If you see everything clearly, you can save a lot of trouble. However, those words are just empty words. How can they resolve the heart of a courtesan who is drifting in the world and infatuated with vain glory? Sure enough, in a short while, Cuiyun came back. She was still as happy and talkative as before. She said that it was not good to eat crabs without eating rice, so let's order some dishes to eat. Zuo Shichen said, "I can't eat rice. Let's buy some porridge to eat." Cuiyun ordered someone to prepare some side dishes for eating with porridge. Zuo Shichen asked her, "You just said you had something to say about Hong Lianxiang. What was it?" Cuiyun said, "That was just to trick you. What else is there to say? After that play, the Yin family spent some money and didn't perform it anymore. Hong Lianxiang's coffin was buried in a piece of land in the countryside of Suzhou. I'm afraid the green grass is already full of it."

Finance: The Gold Market Experienced Frequent Turmoil Last Week 149

Jewish Merchants' Bullish Positions Surged, Reaching Approximately Seven or Eight Thousand Contracts

Small-Sized Short-Term Gold Bars Saw Premiums of Thirteen to Fourteen Taels

As the Autumn Racing Season Approached, Bull and Bear Positions Were Squaring Off, Resulting in Sideways Trading

The silver market, foreign exchange restrictions, and banknotes all saw rising trends. Last week, the state of the gold market was one of sideways trading, with alternating rises and falls and aimless fluctuations. In particular, the industry lacked firm resolve, mainly due to the mutual control exerted by both bull and bear factions. While the silver market and foreign exchange saw slight increases, the gold market ultimately weakened. There were slight shifts from the beginning of the week, but the daily difference reached as high as seven or eight taels. Large bullish positions emerged from Xinheng, the Luo brothers, and others, but signs of weakness were soon revealed, and there seemed to be a potential stabilization towards the weekend, with a difference of four or five taels. Looking back, from Tuesday morning, active sellers suddenly drove the price down to 579 taels. By the next day, due to large players such as Yuansheng and arbitrageurs covering short positions, the price briefly broke through the 590 taels mark, reaching 90 taels and 0.02 yuan. Later, the market became unpredictable and chaotic, with frequent turmoil. Until Saturday, the result was a decline of 2.6 taels compared to the previous Saturday. However, there was also a fluctuation of 11.2 taels during the week. The overall rise in the price of large silver bars was 0.0625, with a range of 0.125. The price of American silver rose 0.125, fluctuating by 0.025 in both directions, while the forward rate rose slightly by half a point, totaling 0.125. The Japanese exchange rate fell by a total of 0.75. The price of bank transactions also loosened, with the forward rate diverging from the spot rate by about 20 taels. It is observed that, as the Southwest Autumn Racing Season approaches, there may be no major changes in the gold market. The general situation over the past week is described in detail below:

Fluctuations of 11 Taels Over the Entire Week: On Monday (October 27), the price of large silver bars contracted, and the exchange rate remained unchanged. The domestic market seemed firm, but Jewish merchants Qiao Rifu and others were selling forward sterling, and the opening gold price was low, at 584.9 taels. Later, due to purchases by Fuchang Yuanheng, Yuanxing Yong, Dadecheng, and others, it reached 87.9 taels. Then, Yuancheng, Jinan, Yu Da, and others tended to sell, suppressing the price by three or four taels. After a flat opening in the afternoon, the market weakened, and the result was 81.7 yuan, a decrease of four taels compared to the previous Saturday. This was due to heavy selling by large players, with a total of about seven or eight thousand short contracts. The next day, the gold market showed improvement. Although the price of large silver bars did not change, the price of silver rose slightly, and the exchange rate trended upwards. Large players squared off positions, and the gold price increased due to bullish leverage. However, the price briefly broke through 80 taels in the morning due to Yu Da, Yuanxing Yong, and others tending to sell. However, large players resumed buying shortly after, and the price turned upwards, reaching 88.7 taels in the afternoon before falling back by three taels. The closing price was 83.5 taels, a decrease of 2.3 taels compared to the previous day. On Wednesday morning, the price increased again. Although the price of large silver bars increased, news of Citibank tending to sell came out, and people's hearts turned upward. There were large players chasing purchases, and the exchange rate was also favorable, soaring to 90.02 taels. Active sellers appeared in the afternoon, and the price fell back by five or six taels. The closing price was 83.5 taels, a decrease of 2.3 taels compared to the previous day. The next day, the silver market did not change, but the exchange rate loosened, and the gold price seemed to weaken, hovering around 84 taels. On Friday, the price of large silver bars did not change, the price of silver rose slightly, and the forward rate rose by half a point. However, the domestic market was flat, with the gold price fluctuating by only four taels, trading little, and fluctuating between 85 taels and 81 taels. On Saturday morning, the price of large silver bars increased, fortunately with good support. The American sale caused the gold market to open high. Then, due to the rush of various firms, it reached 87 taels. Later, sellers became prevalent, and as the Western merchants' autumn racing season next Monday approached, bull and bear positions were largely squared off, so there was only a fluctuation of four taels. However, the market continued to trade sideways, and in the afternoon, it was only at 83.1 yuan, a decrease of 1.1 yuan compared to the previous day. As for the spot price of small-sized gold bars, it seemed to be small, with the short-term price increasing by about thirteen or fourteen taels. However, sales were brisk. Bank Checks Cleared Earlier 152

Today (the 3rd) is the Western merchants' Autumn Racing Season, and banks will be closed in the afternoon as usual. However, the mutual clearing of various silver and foreign currency checks must be done before 11:00 AM. Checks received after 11:00 AM will be processed the next day. Yesterday, the Bank of China notified the money market, stating that the Western merchants' racing season would be from the 3rd to the 5th, and bank checks would only be accepted until 11:00 AM. If various money shops were to clear bank checks, they must be submitted before 10:45 AM in order to have ample time for processing. Please comply. However, Chinese banks that do not close on Saturdays will continue to process transactions as usual.

The State of the World Cotton Industry in the Last Ten Years 157

Decline in Europe and America, Progress in Asia

Since the end of the European War, the cotton spinning industry in various countries around the world has rapidly progressed. Recently, the general decline in world prices has presented a trend of overproduction, which has become increasingly evident recently, especially in Europe and America. Asia, on the other hand, has relatively progressed. The following is a table of the world's spinning machines and raw cotton consumption statistics for the last ten years (unit: thousands):

Year Spinning Spindles Looms Average Consumption per Thousand Spindles Cotton American Cotton (bales)

1913 144,615 2,857 23,000 156

1921 152,317 2,810 17,595 116

1922 154,555 2,831 21,167 137

1923 156,353 2,922 22,143 141

1924 158,462 3,086 20,430 128

1925 161,363 3,111 23,294 144

1926 163,723 3,184 24,681 151

1927 164,597 3,243 25,881 157

1928 165,102 3,278 25,540 155

1929 164,211 3,115 25,882 158

1930 164,120 3,000 25,209 153

Observing the above table, the number of spinning spindles in 1930 was less than in 1927, which shows the declining trend of the cotton spinning industry. It is found that the total number decreased by only 91,000 spindles this year compared to last year, of which Europe decreased by 400,500 spindles and America decreased by 720,000 spindles. However, Asia increased by 972,000 spindles, and other regions also increased by 62,000 spindles, which shows the prevalence of the decline in the European and American spinning industries. Due to various reasons, Asia has made progress. Among them, India increased by 198,000 spindles, Japan increased by 542,000 spindles, and China increased by 227,000 spindles. However, since March, the surge of revolutionary sentiment in India has reduced the work in cotton mills. Japan, due to the lifting of the gold ban and the rise in gold prices, has presented a state of economic recession. Only China, with a decrease in the import of foreign goods, has a relatively good working situation.

The consumption of raw cotton has also decreased due to the unfavorable trade of cotton products. Among them, the decrease in American cotton is particularly large. Other cottons, such as Indian cotton, have seen an increase. The main reason for the consumption of American cotton is that the cotton industry in the Americas is in the most obvious state of decline, and the increase in low-grade products has led to a tendency to substitute cheaper Indian cotton. The efforts of other regions to plant cotton are also sufficient to reduce the use of American cotton. The following is a table of the consumption of various cottons in the last ten years (unit: thousands of 500-pound bales):

Year Total American Cotton Indian Cotton Egyptian Cotton Other

1920 23,000 14,630 3,977 946 3,447

1921 17,595 10,030 4,399 509 2,557

1922 21,167 12,757 5,192 748 2,736

1923 22,143 12,666 5,402 898 3,177

1924 20,430 11,107 5,409 1,028 2,887

1925 23,294 13,256 5,521 970 2,547

1926 24,681 13,731 5,512 921 4,518

1930 25,208 12,023 6,087 937 5,162

The consumption of American cotton in 1930 was very pessimistic, being the lowest figure since 1924. The high consumption of Indian cotton was unprecedented, and the consumption of other cottons was also optimistic. The increased use of domestically grown cotton in China and Russia and the expansion of cotton planting in various countries have resulted in the declining trend of American cotton prices this year. Although this is due to the general decline in prices, the decrease in consumption is actually a major factor. The production of 14 million bales of American cotton is quite appropriate under normal circumstances, but under the current state, it is felt to be too much. And various countries are still working hard to plant cotton. In the future, the dominance of American cotton in the cotton markets of various countries may not be as superior as in the past. Although the government authorities are absorbing new cotton on one hand and advising cotton farmers to reduce planting on the other, in order to increase cotton prices, the general prices are still falling, and cotton farmers will have nowhere to adapt. The low rate of wheat prices has now exceeded cotton prices. It is feared that the effect of farmers abandoning relatively high-priced cotton and switching to cheaper wheat crops will be minimal. The reason for creating this situation is the international economic changes rather than local problems. Only by hoping for the recovery of the economic situation and causing an increase in consumption can the decline in market prices be resolved. According to the estimation of the Lancashire Cotton Corporation, the low point of American cotton prices in 1930-1931 may exceed that of 1929-1930. The following is an estimate of the supply, demand, and market price of American cotton, which is intended to provide a glimpse of future changes.
