The Monument to Martyr Chen Yingshi to Be Inaugurated Today 166

Mr. Chen Yingshi, a martyr of the Kuomintang, tirelessly campaigned for the revolution at the time, and his contribution to the restoration of Shanghai and the Republic of China was truly significant. To establish a permanent memorial to commemorate his achievements, a stone monument was erected outside the Old West Gate on Minguo Road in the Chinese area of this city. After several months of construction, it was completed last month. The towering monument is very majestic. It is scheduled to be inaugurated on the morning of November 3rd (today), and people from all walks of life are invited to attend the opening ceremony. Yesterday, the area around the monument was decorated with colorful flowers, pine trees, and cypresses, which were bright and eye-catching. The entire arrangement was quite spectacular. There should be a lively and grand occasion today.

Mayor Zhang Concerns Himself with the Bereavement Money for the Zhaoeh Martyrs 167

To Be Collected and Distributed by the Municipal Government on Their Behalf

The Zhaoeh Uprising was a major event in the revolutionary process. Regarding the issue of honoring and compensating the martyrs who died in this battle, Mr. Yang Xiaotian, the leader who personally participated in the battle, submitted a request to the National Government for granting official ranks to each martyr and providing preferential treatment to their families. However, the procedures for the family members to receive the compensation were extremely complicated, and it was very difficult for those living in Shanghai to wait. Mayor Zhang of this city, who had followed the late martyr Chen Yingshi in the revolutionary work, was concerned about this and generously took on the responsibility of collecting and distributing the compensation on their behalf. It is reported that the municipal government will directly contact the relevant departments of the central government to ensure that the procedures are expedited and the families of the martyrs are benefited. Upon hearing the news, all the family members were overjoyed.

Yesterday's Public Memorial for Tian Tong 168

Mr. Tian Ziqin of Hubei passed away at sea due to worrying about national affairs, and the whole country mourned. Recently, his younger brother, Jiweijun, and comrades from various provinces in Shanghai, set up a spirit hall at the Chongfa Zen Temple on Gulou Road yesterday to hold a memorial service. More than 1,300 elegiac couplets from the National Government, Chairman Chiang, Hu Zhantang, Li Xiehe, Zhang Yuejun, Zhang Taiyan, Ju Juesheng, and other comrades were hung in front of the spirit hall. The details are recorded below:

The guests who came to the memorial service included Li Xiehe, a member of the Central Supervisory Committee, Zhang Yuejun, a representative of the National Government, and representatives of various legal groups, totaling more than 1,000 people. Mrs. Ju Juesheng, because her husband and Mr. Tian worked together for the party and the country, and now one is dead and one is imprisoned, felt particularly sad and distraught when receiving the guests.

The scene of the public memorial service: At around 11 o'clock, Zhang Yuejun, the mayor of Shanghai, offered a sacrifice on behalf of the National Government, with Xi Chulin, the director of the Department of Customs and Rituals of the Ministry of Interior, assisting in the ceremony, and Xiao Qin, the aide-de-camp of the National Government, reading the eulogy. The eulogy read: "On November 2nd, the nineteenth year of the Republic of China, the National Government sent Zhang Qun, the mayor of Shanghai, to offer a eulogy to the spirit of Mr. Tian Ziqin, a former member of the National Government, saying, 'Alas, Mr. Tian, why did you die so suddenly? Recalling your meritorious deeds, my heart is filled with sorrow. In the old Qing Dynasty, the government was disorganized, and eagles and tigers were watching around. You, at a young age, went to study in Wuchang, spoke boldly about the revolution, and vowed to be generous. You were soon detected and arrested, and fled east to Japan. You were determined to defeat the enemy, and your attitude was激昂. You met heroes, and poured out your heart. You met Sun Yat-sen, and were overjoyed. You joined the Tongmenghui, and planned the Kuang Fu. The wind and clouds rose, and the sea looked forward. You returned to join the righteous army, and your spirit swallowed Hunan. Your extraordinary plan failed, and you stumbled in Pingxiang. You tried again and again, and never rested. You were summoned from ten thousand miles away, and rushed to the coast at night. You were like a trapped phoenix, soaring in the sky. You went north to Yanjing, and traveled south to Nanyang. You vigorously refuted heresies, and our way was彰显. You widely proclaimed the 木铎, and the motherland复光. In the Xinhai Revolution, the Yangtze River was浩浩荡荡, who could resist the fierce enemy? You and 克强. People said you were a scholar, but you were a strategist. Whether you won or lost, you shared the joys and sorrows. You created the Republic of China, and sat in the parliament. You had a pen and a tongue, and your arguments were brilliant. Yuan Shikai's claim to the throne destroyed the great defense. You raised troops on the Huai River, and our martial spirit was扬. Heaven did not regret the disaster, and the atmosphere of bandits was rampant. Great thieves stole the power, and clowns jumped around, following each other, causing disaster to the people. The people's livelihood was ruined, and the public's will was divided. The lofty Sun Yat-sen was great and just, recruiting many talents, and opening the government in Guangzhou. The scale was grand, and the doctrine was正皇. After several dangers, the years passed. Alas, Mr. Tian, you were determined to follow, participating in confidential matters, and supporting the纲常. The righteous army pointed north, sweeping away the tigers and wolves. The benevolent are invincible, and no one dared to resist. The people celebrated the arrival of the army, and the people welcomed them with food and pots. The blue sky and white sun shone with ten thousand feet of light. The capital was in Chongqing, and the government was expanded. You offered advice and assisted the central government. Alas, Mr. Tian, your ambition was pure, your conduct was virtuous, your demeanor was upright, and your mind was vast. You possessed morality, and expressed it in writing. Your voice was loud and substantial, and your voice启蒙. You analyzed the essence and swept away the chaff. You were a teacher for the world, and a 吉祥 for the country. Why did you die so early? The heavens and the earth are vast. Remembering the past, my tears flowed down. Let sincerity be clean, and shine in all directions. May your soul be aware, and I offer this cup of wine. Alas, alas, may you rest in peace.' When the comrades read the eulogy, their voices were sad and mournful, and the guests in the hall were all sorrowful. When Mayor Zhang performed the ceremony, he was touched by the scene and missed his friend, and could not help but feel sad and tearful. From 2 pm, comrades from various provinces and relatives performed public sacrifices in turn, which lasted until late at night."

The Telegram from the National Government: Yesterday, the Tian residence received a telegram from the National Government saying, "Mr. Tian Jiweijun, upon the order of the chairman, the National Government's former member, Mr. Tian Ziqin, will be memorialized in Shanghai on November 2nd. Mayor Zhang Qun of Shanghai is appointed to offer sacrifices on behalf of the government. A separate telegram has been sent to Mayor Zhang. The National Government deeply cherishes the elders, and Mr. Tian's contribution to the party and the country is evident."

The Entire City's Party Members Held a Party Training Contest Final Yesterday 170

The Shanghai Special City Party Department held the final of its first city-wide party member training competition. Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, it took place in the auditorium on the third floor of the department. More than 300 people attended, including representatives from the City Executive Committee Zhu Yingpeng and Fan Zhengbo, Training Minister Tong Xingbai, judges Tao Baichuan, Yang Fayuan, Wu Kaixian (represented by Jiang Huaishu), Wu Xianren, and contestants and guests. The atmosphere was lively and grand. The details of the event are recorded below:

Contestants: Wang Guanyi, Yin Yong, Zhu Aimin, and Zheng Fengchu from District 1; Wang Bin, Lai Zhiwen, Shi Renzhi, Zhou Zenglin, and Yu Xianting from District 2; Xu Zexiang, Gu Jiwu, and Ding Yao Chen Lengseng from District 3; Luo Changmin from District 4; Shen Yu, He Shaoru, and Cui Zhiming from District 5; Jin Guangmei, Li Guohua, Yu Yu, Wang Xiuhe, and Zhang Fucheng from District 6; Yao Zhenlong and Chen Jingqiu from District 7; Pu Hengqing, Li Xiong, and Jin Xihan from District 8; Jin Nianzu from First Direct; Mei Hongying from Second Direct; and guest He Zhushi.

Event Staff: Chairman Tong Xingbai; Judges Zhu Yingpeng, Tong Xingbai, Tao Baichuan, Yang Fayuan, Wu Xianren, Jiang Huaishu; Timekeeper Qin Hegao; Scorer Xu Xingbai; Master of Ceremonies Lu Shujie; Recorder Zhong Weishi; Receptionists Wang Guohua and Huang Tao.

Chairman's Report: Comrades, today is the day we hold the final of the first Shanghai City Party Member Training Competition. Why are we holding this party member training competition? We know that for a party member, cultivation of party ethics, promotion of work, understanding of party principles, and adherence to party discipline are all very important. Currently, we feel that some comrades are gradually neglecting these issues. As a result, when our party comrades go into society and into public groups, they are not making a good impression. To remedy this crisis, we must intensify our training efforts. We have noted that the current party member training work, in addition to holding party congresses, discussions, and lectures, simply has no other methods. Therefore, we often think about how to encourage the spirit of party members and arouse their interest. Only by solving this problem can we hold party member training competitions. We believe that this competition can greatly help train party members in understanding party principles, abiding by discipline, promoting work, and cultivating party ethics. Now, our first final is being held today. The topics set for the first final are all about party ethics because we are preparing to hold three competitions. The purpose of the first competition is to awaken comrades to the cultivation of party ethics. The purpose of the second competition is to promote comrades' understanding of party principles. The purpose of the third competition is to invigorate comrades' spirit for work and instruct them in work methods. Because the meaning is so important, we also strive to be solemn in handling it. All the details have been published in Shanghai newspapers, so there is no need to repeat them. All of you contestants present today are winners from each district and should be fully prepared. However, there are a few points to keep in mind when speaking: 1. The topic of your speech must be selected within the scope specified by the department and must not be determined on your own. 2. The speech time is set at five minutes and must not exceed seven minutes at most. 3. The winners of the final must submit a 2.5-inch portrait photo and a copy of their speech to the department within five days so that they can be compiled into a separate publication for future commemoration. 4. The order of speeches will be based on the order of registration. 5. The competition will be divided into three categories: meaning, eloquence, and demeanor, but slightly more attention will be paid to the meaning aspect, and so on.

Representative's Address: City Executive Committee Representative Comrade Zhu Yingpeng said in his address, "Chairman, comrades, today is the day of the first final of the Shanghai City Party Member Training Competition. The meaning of holding the party member training competition has just been explained in detail by the chairman. We know that the topic of this competition focuses on party ethics because the cultivation of party ethics is indeed the most needed and worthy of attention at present. We see that the discipline and spirit of our party during the period of secret work were better than now. After the party became public, we look at the discipline of our party and the revolutionary personality of our party members. The facts tell us that some party members have gradually neglected the observance of discipline and the cultivation of personality, thinking that being a party member is a special class. This situation is the greatest danger facing our party at present. If this continues, party members will become corrupt day by day, and the discipline of the party will naturally become more and more lax. The training department of this association has recognized this and believes that in order to continue the unfinished mission of the revolution and remedy the current crisis, the first thing to do is to enable all party members to have a very clear understanding of the cultivation of party ethics. We all know very well that we are now in the period of political tutelage, and its work is more serious and difficult than in the military government period. If we ourselves are not sound, how can we gain the trust of the people and how can we realize our principles to complete the national revolution? Therefore, our country believes that this competition can not only stimulate the interest of party members throughout the city in studying party principles but also awaken the attention of party members throughout the city to cultivating party ethics and continuing the new life of our party. All of you comrades are winners of the semi-finals in each district. I hope that today you will give full play to your abilities and encourage each other. I have high hopes for you."

Competition Results: First Place: Jin Guangmei; Second Place: Mei Hongying; Third Place: Li Xiong; Fourth Place: Zheng Fengchu.

Prizes: First Place: A silver shield from the City Executive and Supervisory Committee, a silver shield from the Propaganda Minister, and a silver frame from the Training Minister. Second Place: A silver shield from the City Supervisory Committee and a silver frame from the Organization Minister. Third Place: A silver shield from Standing Committee Member Pan Gongzhan and a silver frame from Standing Committee Member Fan Zhengbo. Fourth Place: A silver frame from the Training Minister and a vertical scroll from Supervisor Zhu Yingpeng.

Reason for Shangguan Yunxiang's Resignation 173

Due to Brain Illness Requiring Long-Term Recuperation

Shangguan Yunxiang, commander of the Ninth Army of the Anti-Rebel Army, commander of the Forty-Seventh Division, and commander of the Pinghan Railway Garrison, made great contributions in the recent campaign to suppress Yan Feng, especially in the advance at Qingxiangji and the victories against the odds at Heti Ridge, Libaji, and the first occupation of Zhengzhou. Recently, it was suddenly heard that his resignation had been approved, which surprised people in society. According to a senior officer at the headquarters, Shangguan had been fighting on the Pinghan and Longhai lines for half a year, with remarkable achievements. However, due to overwork, he suffered a brain injury. After arriving in Zhengzhou, he asked the commander-in-chief for a long vacation, which was not approved. After Chiang returned to Beijing, Shangguan again asked Director He Yingqin for a month's sick leave to recuperate in Hangzhou. The affairs of the army and division headquarters were temporarily handled by Vice Commander Hao Mengling and Chief of Staff Gan Fang. After Shangguan arrived in Hangzhou, doctors diagnosed that he needed long-term recuperation. Following the doctor's advice, he insisted on resigning to Chiang. Chiang could not retain him any longer and had to transfer Shangguan to the position of General Counselor. Wang Jinyu was appointed to fill the vacancy, and Chief of Staff Gan Fang also requested to resign to Chiang at the same time. He has been transferred to the position of Lieutenant General Counselor. Chairman Chiang also instructed the two men to recuperate in peace, and after they recovered, they would be rewarded with important positions.

Gan Jicang, Chief of Staff of the Ninth Army of the Anti-Rebel Army, went to Fenghua to meet Chiang the day before yesterday and presented important official matters in person. Chiang did not receive any guests during this return to Fenghua. However, after Gan arrived in Xikou, Chiang met with him for about an hour before sending him back to Ningbo in a special car. It is said that Gan's trip was to report on internal affairs of the army. According to a close friend of Gan, Gan's trip to Fenghua was because the commander of the army, Shangguan Yunxiang, had a deep brain illness. The doctor told him that he needed a long time to recuperate, Shangguan didn't want to go back to the Ninth Army and entrusted Gan to ask Chiang for leave.

The Second Regiment of the Second Central Training Division stationed in Xu, and the Third Regiment of the Third Division, were ordered to depart the day before yesterday, and yesterday they departed from Beijing on two special trains. Naval Cadets Going to England Arrive in Shanghai 175

The second group of naval cadets sent by the Ministry of the Navy to England, including Han Tingjie, Yang Xitao, Zeng Wanli, Lin Baozhe, students Zhou Botao, Shao Lun, Lu Quanfen, Guo Maolin, and Li Shouyong, arrived in Shanghai from Beijing on the first morning. It is reported that this group of cadets will study English in Shanghai for three months and prepare their luggage. It is expected that they will start their voyage overseas around February next year. After arriving in England, the cadets will enter Greenwich University in London, and the students will be sent to ships for practice. Shanghai-based Hunanese Associations and Relief Societies Jointly Petition 176

Listing Four Key Points

Petition representatives from Hunan in Beijing and Shanghai, because the bandits and communists in Hunan Province are becoming more rampant, and have recaptured Pingliu and Southern China and other counties, are no longer trying to find a fundamental solution. The people of Hunan in deep water and fire will have no survivors. They gathered representatives in Beijing yesterday morning to petition the central government. The text is as follows: "Presenting this to prevent future troubles, we respectfully request the dismissal of He Jian, Chairman of the Hunan Provincial Government and Commander-in-Chief of the Four Routes, to stabilize Hunan Province and consolidate the foundation of the country. We believe that He Jian is greedy, stubborn, false, and reckless, causing repeated disasters. The fellow villagers' associations in the subordinate provinces, Beijing, Shanghai, Guangdong, and Hubei have repeatedly stated his crimes of harming the country and harming the people, and pleaded for punishment to seek a good aftermath. It has already been meticulously documented. Our Central Government is broad-minded and wants to observe the results later, and it also happens to be the time when the campaign against rebellion is urgent, and it is difficult to transfer divisions and brigades. Now that the glory has been restored and the troops are returning south, it is not difficult to quell the banditry by encircling and searching. However, the joy of peace is not only relying on military power to succeed, and the addition of great responsibilities is definitely not something that mediocre people like He Jian can handle. Now, based on what the representatives of various groups in Hunan Province hope for in the joint meeting resolution, we want to use the intention of punishing the past to prevent future troubles to seek a timely way to manage the country. We dare not bother you, but only list the items for our Lord to respectfully present to you. 1. Please punish He Jian to maintain discipline. It has been found that He Jian has long been accustomed to the deception of the rebel Tang Shengzhi. His possession of his current position originally came from secretly colluding with the Gui faction to squeeze out the former post, fearing punishment and surrendering, which was added with the elimination and aid. When Tang rebelled in Zheng, He Jian harbored two ambitions and dared to advocate the maintenance of the territory and the people under the great unification. He was feudal, arbitrary, independent, and unscrupulous, inherited the bad habits of the warlord era, and would have made the party and the country more chaotic if Heaven had not hastened Tang's demise. This year, Yan Feng rebelled together, Zhang Guiheng was connected, He Jian gathered representatives from the north and south in Changsha, and there were secret telegram exchanges almost every day. He cared about the cloud man in the sky, and he was infatuated with the flying wild goose. He did not know the corruption of his subordinates, and he did not see the prevalence of bandits, which led to the capture of both Gui and bandits, and the disasters were overwhelming. Xianyang was half burned, the Guanzhong area was depleted, Wuhan was shaken, and the overall situation was swaying. To this day, bandits and robbers are still rampant in various parts of eastern Hunan, trapped in water and fire, and He Jian can't come up with a solution. He only reports falsely and embellishes his achievements after the bandits retreat. The foundation of the country, discipline is the first priority. If the central government still shows extraordinary tolerance to such a person who is self-interested in owning troops and is fickle and unpredictable, it will make those who are loyal to the party and the country feel discouraged, and those who seize the opportunity to seek profit will become more and more self-centered. Punishing He Jian is what all the people of Hunan Province, regardless of their wisdom, old age, or youth, are earnestly striving for. 2. Please improve the organization of the Hunan Provincial Government. It has been found that the Hunan Provincial Government has suffered from various shortcomings in its organization due to He Jian's incompetence. We dare not make specific accusations here, but we must learn from the past. Therefore, we must seek appropriate people to succeed him. The power to employ people is in the hands of the central government and is not something that the people should interfere with. However, the virtue of talents is related to the governance of the country, and it is also related to the well-being of the people. They are all connected, and they cannot help but hope to get people. We believe that the selection of the chairman should not be a soldier in active service. The Hunan situation has repeatedly arisen from He Jian's control of military power, not to wholeheartedly defend the people, but to monopolize power. Recently, Chen Mingshu, chairman of Guangdong, wrote an article saying that military and political affairs should be separated and should not be given to soldiers in active service, and that the governance of the province should be rewarded to military mediocre. This has always been regarded as the golden rule of politics in ancient history and in the present world. Moreover, our country is now inheriting the bad habit of warlord autocracy. How great are the words, the trajectory of peace. However, in the autumn of chaos and harmony, there are also difficult places to integrate. At this time, the country is in trouble, and the mountains are full of thieves. How easy is it to disarm and repair literature? Today's military knowledge must belong to those who are familiar with research. Then, it is not a soldier in active service, but he must have the ability to command military affairs to be able to cope with the current environment, which is also a necessary condition. However, in our Hunan government, in addition to the chairman, almost half of the provincial committees are soldiers in active service, and many of them are remote and do not hold positions. This is why it is difficult to govern. To govern, we must understand politics. However, He Jian, who has been in power for two years, has no achievements to mention. It is difficult to record his party and government. We must also have a political mind and the determination to clarify official administration, rectify finances, and eliminate bandits. After the great disaster in Hunan, everything is chaotic. How can we seek peace and stability, how can we recuperate, and how can we clear up? If we are not familiar with the situation, we will inevitably have the feeling of closing the door and building a car. As for whether the person is trusted by the central government, admired by the people of Hunan, expands the party's principles, and has a deep historical understanding of the revolutionary process, it is a common qualification. He Jian's heart is rebellious, and our central government is tired of driving, which is why he lacks this qualification. 3. Please thoroughly eliminate bandits and communists. He Jian has spent huge sums of money on cleaning up the countryside, but he has ended up with the disaster of burning and killing. Tracing back to the cause, one is due to embellishment and perfunctory, and the other is due to ignoring the people's groups. Now that the great disaster has been quelled, our central government has a large-scale bandit suppression plan to save our people from the disaster. This is like a accumulated tumor. Military force can only cut and treat it, and disinfection and muscle growth depend on the government to treat bandits and improve local defense, and promote autonomy. This is an urgent task. However, rectifying the officialdom, clarifying the administration, maintaining the wealth of the people, and transforming people's hearts are necessary conditions for thorough elimination. This has the closest relationship with renewing the organization of the provincial government and is what our people are praying for day and night. 4. Please order He Jian to cancel illegal surcharges and reduce the burden on the people. We have found that the Hunan Province's annual income and expenditure in the 18th year can be offset. He Jian used the excuse of rehabilitation, and the military committee decided to collect a rehabilitation donation of 8 million yuan. There are three types of donations: 1. field rent donation and lake field mu donation, 2. business capital donation, 3. county town and urban area house donation. Special commissioners were sent to various counties to urge the collection, which was as urgent as a starfire. This surcharge on the people was neither reported to the government for approval nor decided by the provincial government meeting.

Page 14

It is in great conflict with Articles 2 and 5 of the Provincial Government Organization Law promulgated by the government, as well as the repeated orders to cancel surcharges and taxes. His contempt for the law and disregard for the central government have reached such an extent that he should be ordered to cancel He Jian immediately to comply with the orders. Then the people of Hunan will be grateful. 5. Set up a method to help the victims of the disaster. The areas that have been repeatedly affected by bandits are even worse than the battlefield. Burning and destruction are everywhere, and deaths are common. The chickens and dogs in the villages have been destroyed. The boundaries of the fields have also been lost. They are displaced on the roads and ditches. Families are broken, and there is nowhere to rely on. Therefore, I don’t know how many people have died of hunger and disease. Now, the winter solstice is approaching, which will add to the killing cold. He Jian does not seek to save them, but still imposes his surcharges and miscellaneous taxes on our people, as if he is afraid that the people will not be difficult enough, and to increase the current number. Our central government is diligent in consoling the people and is currently trying to provide relief in the battlefield. It has also approved 100,000 yuan for our Hunan. The people of Hunan are deeply grateful. We should ask to issue it as soon as possible or send someone to comfort them, or hand it over to the gentry of Hunan Province to handle it. It is heard that dozens of refugees die every day in the Lushan area, and there are even more scattered. This is an urgent policy to be implemented. He Jian can't be waited for, so we have to look up to the central government. Although what has been presented above belongs to standard governance, it is actually the capital affair. I hope that the Lord will humbly listen and carefully examine the opinions of the people. He will use his natural virtue to benefit the people and create happiness for the people of Hunan. The decisive policy is to punish He Jian first. I am fortunate to have the thought of going out of office and waiting for the order. I am frightened and prolong my eagerness. Republic of China, Year 19.

Yancheng and Funing Fellow Villagers Association Urges to Save the Countryside 177

Submitting a Document to the Provincial Government

The Preparatory Committee of the Yancheng and Funing Fellow Villagers Association in Shanghai, because the two counties of Yancheng and Funing have been severely hit by bandits, and the people are in dire straits, sent a document to the provincial government yesterday, asking for the government's (hall) attention to the situation and to quickly clean up the countryside and find a way to provide relief. "We repeatedly saw reports and received letters and telegrams from our hometown, knowing that my Yancheng and Funing have been hit by the disaster of bandit Ma Yuren, who burned, looted, and scattered the tombs and mounds. The strong were scattered in all directions, and the old and weak turned into ditches. The villages were scorched earth, and there was no place to live. Those who saw it were sad, and those who heard it were also sad. Although there are provincial police teams to fight them hard, they are only hiding and ambushing, which is not a thorough solution. If you want to cut grass and remove roots, one, you must quickly clean up the countryside, just like the overturning of the nest does not leave its eggs, so that you can permanently eliminate bandits. Second, you must restore the people's regiments, especially the joint defense, so that bandits can be wiped out at any time and are not easy to produce. Third, the guns captured by the provincial police team are the ones that Ma Yuren and the people robbed from the people, because the people's regiments cannot be in joint defense, so it is difficult for the few to fight against the many. For the sake of the present, the guns will be returned to the people's regiments, and they will be strictly trained and united with the group. The bandits will also be frightened. The above are all about eliminating the disaster. As for the relief part, four, such as quickly allocating provincial funds to relieve the old and young in Yancheng and Funing from the plight of being displaced, hungry and cold, if you do not quickly set up a method, then the dead will die and the survivors will also die. This is indeed a matter that cannot be delayed for a moment. Fifth, please exempt this year's winter transportation, because the officials come from the people and the people come from the soil. Now, the people who rely on the soil for their livelihood have been trampled on. Although you want to dig and dig, you can't get it in the end, so you have to exempt the winter transportation. Sixth, please investigate and seal Ma Yuren's rebellious property as soon as possible and use it for local charity needs, such as using the profits to make small businesses, such as relief centers or vocational training centers, so that the helpless poor people will not end up starving to death, and then gradually restore the vitality of my Yancheng and Funing. The above are all about relieving the poor. We are deeply saddened by our hometowns and appeal to you. I think that you will take the heart of hunger and drown and follow the footsteps of benevolence and righteousness. I sincerely hope that you will examine and implement it, which is a virtue. I am respectfully presenting this to Ye, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and Hu, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs.

Declaration of the Tea Industry Association 184

Our country's tea, due to its excellent quality and taste, has always been praised by the world. Therefore, it occupies an important position in foreign markets. During the most prosperous era, the annual export value was as high as over 50 million customs taels. However, due to tea merchants adhering to old methods and not knowing how to improve, foreign markets have been almost entirely occupied by new tea-producing countries such as England and Japan in recent years, resulting in a gradual decline in export volume. In addition, the right to foreign trade is entirely controlled by foreign merchants, who manipulate prices and engage in various forms of extortion, causing tea merchants to suffer losses and go bankrupt, which is common. Recently, tea merchants Li Jingming, Dan Shoufu, Hu Songpu, Cheng Baozhang, Yu Jin, Wang Sipu, and others initiated an industry association to discuss methods of maintaining the industry. The declaration of the association is transcribed below:

Declaration: Chinese tea is a natural specialty. The tea produced in Anhui is particularly excellent in flavor and aroma, surpassing all others in the world. Unfortunately, operators in this industry have no solidarity and cannot directly export to foreign countries, resulting in repeated failures. Today, the situation has become irreversible. Historically, Russian merchants were the largest consumers. They used to buy directly from our country. Russians, knowing the quality of our products, did not hesitate to pay high prices for transportation. In the past, "Xichun" teas were valued at 100 taels. Since the breakdown of relations between China and Russia, trade has stopped. Our tea merchants did not think of finding ways to change production or find new outlets, leading to the abandonment of the teas and financial losses. This has led people to believe that "Xichun" teas have no other market, encouraging price manipulation. Therefore, the [unclear] association [unclear] intentionally suppresses prices. Initially, first grade "Xichun" teas were still priced at 80-90 taels, and second grade at 50-60 taels. Later, due to the government suspecting Russian merchants of communist tendencies and detaining them in Hankou, trade was temporarily suspended. Our tea merchants were frightened, and the Russians became deeply aware of this. In reality, Russian consumption did not decrease as a result. It only strengthened the resolve to manipulate prices. Recently, they have even lowered the price to over 20 taels. Where can one operate under these conditions? The [Russian] assistance association is the most difficult for our tea industry to deal with. The British, French, and other countries arbitrarily cut prices, even delaying weighing and slow to pay, using false defaults to extort, which is common. There is no reason for the delays, and the unexpected suffering is unbearable. If we do not take immediate action to remedy the situation, not only will our tea firms have no income, but tea farmers will also face ruin. Furthermore, with banditry rampant in the interior, transportation is obstructed, and the tea-producing areas are scattered, making it impossible to transport tea-making materials. Whether we can operate next year is a major problem. We have thought long and hard and decided to conduct a thorough investigation of existing stocks. If this year's stocks are estimated for next year, we will separate the remaining teas according to quality, estimate the price fairly, and determine the lowest level. If foreign firms still want to reduce the price, we must not agree. We will wait for guarantees to be issued next year and promote to the tea-producing areas the production of Mao Feng, Yuqian, and Hong Qing teas for sale to local stores. Next year, we will prepare to suspend foreign trade and wait for opportunities. At the same time, we will petition the government to find other relief measures. If the government cannot provide relief, we will have no choice but to cease operations. This year's market price has fallen to such a low level. Based on this market price as the standard for tea operations, there is no way to operate next year. Moreover, according to recent estimates, the price has fallen again and again. Not to mention the cost of tea production, even the transportation costs are insufficient. For example, "Xiumei" teas are estimated at 9 or 10 taels. As for "Xichun" teas, they are estimated at over 40 taels. "Tuzhuang Zhenmei" teas are estimated at over 30 taels, and "Luzhuang Zhenmei" teas are 10 or 20-30 taels lower. The price of Qining black tea is even lower. These figures are alarming. If prices are further reduced, with "Xichun" teas at 20 taels and "Zhenmei" teas falling another 10 or 20 taels, the firm's capital will certainly be lost, and the pawnshops will also suffer. This is true for those with weak capital. Those with strong capital may also be wiped out. In short, if we cannot obtain a reasonable price for this year's teas and sell them gradually, then we must not collect scraps next year and try our luck. One attempt will lead to a flood of new and old stock, inevitably repeating the current mistakes. Since we are suffering today, let us not sacrifice ourselves next year. We hope that our tea merchants will wake up, maintain our existing strengths, and develop solidarity for future growth. This will be enough to remedy the situation. We are currently investigating the number of Luzhuang teas imported this year and the estimated number. The remaining Zhenmei, Xichun, and other teas are not sufficient to meet next year's sales volume, so there is no fear of being suppressed due to excess goods. Furthermore, we will let foreign merchants know that we are prepared and will not be suppressed again. We are now offering our humble opinion to our colleagues and have scheduled a general meeting for all members on November 9 at the Foreign Trade Association. This matter concerns the overall situation and still requires public discussion. If anyone has a great idea, please express it on the spot and let the public vote. This is an announcement.

Municipal Chinese Medicine Association Held General Meeting the Night Before Last 185

Discussing the Issue of Full Merger of Three Organizations

The Shanghai Municipal Chinese Medicine Association held a general meeting at its new association located at 275 Zhejiang Road, Yizhong Company, on the second floor the night before last. Preparatory committee members present included Xue Wenyuan, Ding Zhongying, Zhu Shaowu, Yu Hongsun, Cheng Diren, and nineteen others. Xie Liheng was publicly elected chairman, and Jiang Wenfang recorded the proceedings. The chairman first reported that 1) membership in the association had reached 1,237 people in the past two months, and the general membership meeting was scheduled for the 10th of this month; 2) member [unclear] Xiaoyan was wrongly accused. The association's certification had already led the Health Bureau to return his license and the Provisional Court to dismiss the prosecution; 3) member [unclear] Yuting reported being obstructed in his business, and the association had investigated and the offending person had provided a written apology; 4) the association had jointly hosted Mr. Fairbairn with various organizations, and he had expressed satisfaction with the Chinese Medical College established by the association; 5) the [People's] Council had issued a clear order for the Shenzhou, Zhonghua, and Chinese Medicine three organizations to cease activities and merge into the association. The attendees were asked to report on the opinions of the various organizations. Jiang Wenfang stated that Shanghai's Chinese medicine community has historically had the organization of three bodies. Continuing that they have felt the need for concentrated unification, they formed this association, while the three groups still engaged in the same objectives and duties. They avoided power and rights, so the strength of the group reduced invisible. The enterprise of Chinese medicine was not easy to progress, resulting in suppression of the Ministry of Civil Affairs. It can be especially regreted now that most of the groups members are in favor of the merger, to avoid duplicated efforts. Bao Shibing said that Chinese medicine community groups were formed solely to seek public service development. Merger would have a strong power. As the initiator of Shenzhou, the presiding over association affairs for the longest time, he knew the Shenzhou commission would be aware of the implications. Chuan Yongyan said that a union is effective, a separation is ineffective. Zhu Hegao said that in the past few days, he had investigated the opinions of 150 members of each organization and found that the Zhonghua Chinese Medicine and other groups did not hold a single meeting throughout the year and were controlled by one or two people. The membership was thus extremely eager to merge. The funds held by each organization amounted to over 20,000 yuan, but most of them were lost and difficult to close. Zhang Zanchen said that the committee members of this association were mostly committee members of the three organizations, so why separate and create more committee titles, which cost more membership money. Xia Zhongguang said that from the standpoint of a party member, organizations that did not comply with orders could not establish committees, and members who did not comply with party orders could not engage in group activities and would be subject to punishment. Next, the discussion of the proposals began. Proposal 1: Should we welcome the merger of the three Chinese medicine organizations into this association? 1. The Chinese Medicine Club established by the association will invite committee members from the three organizations to hold a joint meeting on the afternoon of the 5th at 5:00 PM. 2. Members of each organization who join this association before the general meeting will be exempt from membership fees. 3. Extend the date of the general meeting so that new members have voting rights. 4. The employees hired by the three organizations have served the Chinese medicine community for a long time. Now that activities have ceased, this association should send a letter of invitation to join the work of this association. Proposal 2: The association should immediately notify the members who serve the work of the three organizations to cease activities to avoid violating party orders. Resolved: Passed. Proposal 3: The association should immediately notify all Chinese medicine practitioners in the city to clarify the truth. Resolved: The association's editorial committee will handle. Proposal 4: How should the association handle the merger issue of the three Chinese medicine organizations? Resolved: Each organization should first close down on its own. That evening, 28 committee members from the three organizations, including Shen Xinjiu, Huang Baozhong, Xu Shoupeng, and others, gathered at the Chinese Medicine Club and unanimously signed a statement urging the standing committees of the three organizations to expedite the closure. It was later learned that the six standing committee members of the three organizations were holding a meeting at a certain medical residence in Beining [unclear] Bridge and decided that the chairman [unclear] would send a letter urging them to comply with the order to merge and not to act rashly, lest they make repeated mistakes, respect public opinion, and maintain the overall situation together.

Coal Industry Petitions the Ministry of Railways to Promptly Order Railway Bureaus to Protect Domestic Coal 186

Maintain the Reduced Coal Transportation Rates on the Jiaoji Railway

The Coal Industry Association petitions the Ministry of Railways to request the maintenance of the reduced coal transportation rates on the Jiaoji Railway: Because the Jiaoji Railway Bureau has cancelled the original reduced coal transportation rates, which is confirmed to hinder the development of domestic coal and promote the sale of foreign coal, we respectfully present the reasons and request your review and approval to maintain the old rules and allocate more coal transportation vehicles to alleviate the coal shortage and protect domestic production. The areas along the Jiaoji Railway, such as Boshan and Zichuan in Shandong Province, are all coal-producing areas. In addition to supplying the province for consumption, a large amount is transported and exported annually by the Jiaoji Railway. Currently, the import of foreign coal is increasing daily, and domestic coal is hindered by the war and transportation is stagnant. Only Boshan and Zichuan can load and export from Qingdao, which is only a slight resistance. Examining the Shanghai Customs import trade register, the item of foreign coal reaches tens of millions of yuan annually. Such outflow of profits is not trivial. Blocking the leak is the urgent task of our country today. The original regulations of the Jiaoji Railway stipulated that export transportation costs for domestic coal would be reduced by half. This method is a major plan to promote domestic coal and resist foreign goods. The law is good and the intention is beautiful, which is beneficial to the national economy and the people's livelihood. However, it has not had a huge effect because 1) the methods of mining and coal mining have not been improved, resulting in excessive costs and the inability to compete with foreign coal, and 2) there is a lack of vehicles, which cannot fully meet the transportation needs. The coal from Boshan transported to other ports relies entirely on the halved transportation costs, so that producers and merchants can survive. If the reduced rates are abolished, the cost of domestic coal will increase suddenly. Not only will coal merchants be deterred, but the mined coal will inevitably pile up on the mountains, and the completed mines will inevitably be shut down. The livelihood of hundreds of thousands of workers will also be cut off as a result. The opportunity for foreign coal to invade will expand. The harm to the national economy and the people's livelihood cannot be described in words. If the railway authorities want to increase revenue, they should prepare more vehicles for transportation, which is the best policy. If the original reduced rates are abolished, the transportation rate will inevitably decrease revenue and retreat, and the desire to benefit will turn to loss. Now that the military affairs have been pacified, the original state has gradually recovered, and the mines and coal can be mined as much as possible. In addition to supplying domestic needs, it can be exported in large quantities to resist foreign coal. This is the common hope of the people, to block the leak and expand rights, and to seek national wealth and promote people's livelihood. The National Railway has the obligation to facilitate domestic goods and support domestic coal. Reading Dr. Sun Yat-sen's National Construction Strategy and industrial policy, the development of domestic coal is listed as an important plan. Our government will maintain and support it. How can we abolish the benefit transportation method? It seems to conflict with the party's righteousness and government orders. Therefore, we dare to express our foolish sincerity and petition your ministry to review and promptly order the railway bureau to maintain the old rules, support domestic coal, increase the number of vehicles, and transport as much as possible to benefit the country and the people. We feel the danger and dare not be silent. We dare to express our humble words and hope for your understanding and approval to implement, which is for the public good.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sends Letter Requesting Admonition of Loan Rent Collectors 188

Recent Housing Donation Tickets Should Be Used as the Standard

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Municipal Finance Bureau stating that it received a letter from the local blacksmith association on the 20th of this month, stating that the loan rent collectors came to the meeting yesterday to collect rent for the month of January, saying that the assessed rent was 60 yuan. [The blacksmith association] immediately replied that the assessed rent did not match, but the collector insisted on collecting the full amount on the 31st of this month. [The Municipal Chamber of Commerce] examined the quarterly housing donation ticket which indicated the rent was 45 silver yuan per month. It has since submitted the autumn housing donation ticket and request a reply from the Finance Bureau with transfer to the collection office for loaning the monthly rent of 45 yuan, as stated in the donation ticket. Enclosed is the donation ticket. Article 7 of the Shanghai Revenue Short-Term Treasury Bill Loan Rent Regulations states that the rent for each household should be based on the amount listed on the most recent housing donation ticket. The autumn housing donation receipt of the association, Huangzi No. 15249 in the southern district, clearly states the monthly rent is 45 silver yuan. The landlord must pay an autumn donation of 6 yuan and 75 cents. The rent collector should collect a fixed amount of 45 yuan per month, but he arbitrarily increased the price to 60 yuan, which is a violation of the regulations and is akin to illegal collection. The association previously reported that the paint industry association reported that the collectors in the district also did not follow the amount on the donation ticket and arbitrarily increased the price for collection. A letter was sent on the 27th of this month to request investigation and obstruction. Up to the point of another report by the public association of a former situation, the assessment suggests the collectors in each district are not able to act by law. As a response, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce submits a letter and requests to notify this district to act in accordance with the law. On the other hand, it asks that there be a strict admonition for all district collectors.

Zhabei Military Garment Factory Fire: Over a Hundred Workers' Cries Shook the Heavens 190

Most of the Hundred-Plus Workers Were Burned

Approximately Four or Five People Died in the Fire

Factory Buildings, Military Garments, and Machinery Were Reduced to Ashes

The Third Factory of Fuchang Military Garments, located on Gonghe Road in Zhabei, suddenly caught fire due to carelessness at 3:50 PM yesterday. Over a hundred workers in the factory were mostly burned, and approximately four or five lost their lives. The number of those temporarily unaccounted for is not included. The total loss of materials, military uniforms, machinery, and buildings is estimated to be around 30,000 yuan. The fire started at 3:50 PM and was extinguished by 5:30 PM. Ten multi-story buildings and five single-story buildings were all reduced to ashes.

The Fuchang Military Garment Third Factory, specializing in manufacturing military uniforms, is a branch established by the Fuchang Company on the Hongqiao pier outside the Broadway Road in the Public Concession. It originally dealt in woolen fabrics but later switched to military uniforms. Recently, due to business development, it established Factories One and Two on Shanyang Road and Gonghe Road in Zhabei at the end of August this year, specializing in military uniforms. Although the Third Factory on Gonghe Road is temporary, it employs a large number of workers. The first batch of cotton military uniforms was 40,000 sets. Recently, it also bid to the Nanjing General Headquarters and undertook a large number of military uniforms. Therefore, the main factory and the first and second branches all started working day and night to rush the new uniforms.

Sudden Fire: The Third Branch, which caught fire yesterday due to carelessness, is located at No. 209 at the intersection of Gonghe Road and Huakang Road in Zhabei. It was originally a weaving factory, later rented by Baolin to establish a cotton factory. At the end of August this year, it was subleased to Fuchang. The factory building consists of ten multi-story buildings and five single-story buildings. Fuchang Military Garment Factory rented five single-story buildings and five bays of the multi-story buildings along Gonghe Road. The rest was used by Baolin's waste cotton factory. Yongting and Jintai also set up within. The workers employed by the Fuchang Military Garment Factory are all female workers, about a hundred people, and only more than ten male workers. Yesterday at around 3:50 PM, a shout was suddenly heard in the cotton fluffing room, shouting fire alarm. Hearing the alarm, all the workers were frightened and ran for their lives.

The Fire Was Very Fierce: Cotton is originally flammable, and the cotton used in military uniforms has been treated to be light, loose, and dry, making it even more flammable. Therefore, after carelessness in the cotton fluffing room downstairs, it spread up and down in a moment, and the fire tongues spread in all directions. The entire factory building was filled with smoke and flames. In an instant, order was in great chaos, and the female workers were calling for help and shouting wildly, with no solution. In addition, most people were upstairs. Hearing the fire alarm, they all rushed to escape down the stairs. There were too many people and the stairs were small, unable to descend. Therefore, countless people were burned.

Difficult to Extinguish: After the fire broke out, the fire brigades from various sections of Zhabei drove to the scene to extinguish the fire. The fire brigade of Section One arrived at the scene especially early. No less than a dozen fire engines arrived at the scene, trying their best to put out the fire. However, there were as many as 250 bales of cotton stored in the factory, and there were also about seventy or eighty military uniforms that had been made. After the fire, cotton wool was flying everywhere, chain burning, so that there was fire everywhere. Even with a hundred jets of water, it was difficult to save. Moreover, the building of the factory was also old, decayed and withered, and would fall down at a touch. Therefore, it was not easy to spray water on the one hand and rescue the factory workers on the other.

Mostly Burned: Nine out of ten workers in the factory are female workers. When they worked, they often brought their children to play. Therefore, there were also many children in the factory. After the fire, mothers looked for their daughters, fathers looked for their sons, and the cries shook the sky. Except for those who were downstairs and strong, who were able to escape through the door nearby, seventy or eighty percent were burned by the flames. Fortunately, the firefighters tried their best to put out the thick flames gradually, and on the one hand, ordered the workers to break out of the fire, but sixty or seventy people had been burned and fell and injured.

Crying to the Hospital: The female workers who were burned by the fire shouted and screamed in pain for a while, at a loss. Fortunately, the Xinmin Road Pushan Hospital was not far away. Therefore, those who could still walk all shouted and cried with injuries to the Pushan Hospital for help. The doctors in the hospital initially saw only six or seven people arriving and thought that the fire was still light. Who knew that during the bandaging and treatment, three or four groups later came in disarray, countless, crying and crying, which was very pitiful. Therefore, Dr. Zhu and others supervised the assistants to take care of the treatment in order, no less than sixty people before and after.

A Glimpse of the Deaths and Injuries: The fire was extinguished around 5:30 PM. The number of those burned to death and scorched to death was temporarily impossible to investigate. However, in addition to the more than sixty people who went to Pushan Hospital for treatment, the rest were sent by the Public Security Bureau Fire Brigade and other hospitals to the Red Cross Hospital, Baolong Hospital, Renji Hospital, and Guangren Hospital for treatment. The known deaths are as follows: two in Pushan Hospital, one in the Red Cross Hospital, Chen Kashi and Wang Cailin in Baolong Hospital. The hospitalized: Zhu Shunzhi, Yong person, twelve years old in Renji Hospital, Wang Cailin, Jiangbei, fourteen years old in Baolong Hospital, Gu Yu Shi, thirty-three years old, Menghe person, Li Hu Shi, thirty-two years old, Xuzhou person, Ye Yu Shi, forty-three years old, Yong person, Yuan Zhu Shi, forty-six years old, Shaoxing person, her daughter five years old, and four others were sent to Qianyi Trauma Hospital, all women.

Police Suppression: When the fire broke out, the police from the Fourth District Public Security Bureau dispatched many police officers to the fire scene to suppress it, and arrested Zhang Caihua, supervisor of the related Fuchang Military Garment Factory, Liang Youfang, inspector, and Yu Duanfu and Bao Guohan of Baolinji Waste Cotton Factory and other factory management personnel to the district office for interrogation. The manager of Fuchang Military Garment Factory is Wu Desheng from Fenghua, and the founder of Baolinji is Bao Linshu from Yong. When the fire broke out, they were not at the scene. Only part of the two factories has fire insurance.

A Glimpse of the Fire Scene: The burned area is not very wide, at the intersection of Gonghe Road and Huakang Road, next to the old site of the Fourth District Branch Security Bureau in Zhabei. The reporter went to watch after the fire was extinguished. At that time, the smell of burned cotton rushed into the nose. The firefighters were all busy working. The short walls and bamboo fences along the street had all collapsed and were burned. Bricks and tiles and withered wood were piled on the ground. Cotton and military uniforms were all gone. Only a gunpowder room at the entrance of the factory was fortunately not affected when the fire broke out, otherwise the huge loss and the intensity of the disaster would be unimaginable.

Smuggling Chinese into America, Commonly Known as "Hiding Yellow Fish" 191

Li Zaichen Had "Hiding Yellow Fish" Behavior

Extorted 4,000 Yuan by Thugs

Li Zaichen, a Ningbo person and steward of the American merchant ship "Xuefupai" (transliteration), was coerced by Wang Fucai, the head of the sailors on the ship, using threats at 8:00 AM on the 30th of last month. Wang, with his gang, took Li to Room 13 of the Ningbo Hotel at No. 19 Dongxinqiao Street in the French Concession, extorting 4,000 yuan on false pretenses. After the case was exposed, the Chinese detectives Feng Qi, Liu Junjie, and Shen Dehui from the Hongkou Police Station arrested Wang Fucai and his accomplice, Xu Lihui, a Ningbo person, at the Taiping Wharf outside Hongqiao on Broadway Road at around 10:00 AM the next morning. The former morning, they were escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the Special Zone Court. According to the statement of the case by Zhang Tianyin, the lawyer of the police station, according to American law, all Chinese who want to study or do business in the United States must obtain a passport from the US Consulate before they can land, otherwise they will be rejected. If they land secretly, they must be dealt with in accordance with the Immigration Law. After the term expires, the Chinese will be sent back to their home country. The plaintiff privately took many Chinese to the United States, without ship fees and without passports, secretly landing and obtaining a lot of money. This kind of behavior is commonly known as "hiding yellow fish", and the defendant Wang Fucai knew this and used this "hiding yellow fish" as a reason to extort the plaintiff. If the plaintiff really had such a thing, then he would also violate the immigration law of the country. Later, Chinese detectives Liu Junjie and others stated one after another that when arresting Wang Fucai, they saw many thugs gathered there. Later, the plaintiff pointed out that Xu Lihui was also present at the Ningbo Hotel when he was defrauded, so he was arrested and other words. According to the plaintiff Li Zaichen, he was a steward on the American ship Xuefupai, and the defendant Wang Fucai was a colleague. The ship arrived in Shanghai at 2:00 PM on the 30th of last month. After unloading the goods, I went ashore at 5:00 PM and went to the Hua general manager's office in Room 99 of the Dadong Hotel to report everything. After a while, Wang Fucai came and invited me out for dinner. Just out of the hotel door, I was coerced by him with many thugs to the Ningbo Hotel in the French Concession and extorted 10,000 yuan. His accomplice, Zhu Heshang, took out a pistol to threaten me, saying at least 4,000 yuan, otherwise he would dig out my eyes. I had no choice but to agree. I paid 200 yuan first, and made a note for the balance, and agreed to pay the money at the Taiping Wharf on Broadway Road the next morning. After I escaped, I went to the Hongkou Police Station to report and send detectives to arrest him and so on. Wang Fucai claimed that the plaintiff had asked him to go to Huashunlai Law Firm at No. 20 Jiya Lane, Daigou Bridge at about 7:00 PM on that day to negotiate. When he went there to wait for the plaintiff, he did not meet him. At about 8:00 PM, he received a phone call saying that he was in Room 99 of the Dadong Hotel. I went there and talked a few words with him, and went to Zhu Heshang's place in Room 13 of the Ningbo Hotel in the French Concession to settle the yellow fish money. Because the plaintiff had brought a total of 18 Cantonese people to the United States to work before leaving Shanghai, and when the ship arrived at the American wharf, he arranged for 8 people to land. The remaining 10 people could not get their wish and were brought back to Shanghai. I know that he made a lot of money. Each person who landed was 1,450 yuan, totaling more than 10,000 yuan. I partnered with him in this yellow fish business. When the ship returned to Shanghai, he was on the ship and had already promised to give me 4,000 yuan, so I settled the account with him at the Ningbo Hotel, and there was no extortion with thugs. The 200 yuan mentioned by the plaintiff was also not received, and Zhu Heshang did not threaten with a pistol, etc. Xu Lihui's statement was ambiguous. The plaintiff Li Zaichen denied privately taking 18 Cantonese people to the United States. However, there were indeed 10 Chinese people brought back when the ship arrived in Shanghai this time. The 10 people were detained by the US Immigration Bureau and had no passports, so they were sent back to their country. After I was suspected of this, I have already resigned to the shipping company. The defendant's agent, lawyer Fan Gang, stated that the two parties were actually arguing over the yellow fish fee, not extortion. Therefore, he requested that the defendant be allowed to be released on bail pending trial. Judge Ge Zhiqin verified the confession and ordered the defendant Wang Fucai to be remanded, Xu Lihui to pay 1,000 yuan bail, and reschedule the hearing for further verification.

Wharf Thugs Forcibly Demanding Toll Money 192

Three People Arrested

Tang Jihua, alias Yujun, a Ningbo person from Zhejiang, was a staff member of the First Section of the Qingdao Municipal Government. He asked for leave to return home. After finishing his business, he took the Xin Ningshao steamboat to Shanghai in Ningbo. Yesterday morning at about 7:00 AM, after the boat arrived in port, Tang took a number of luggages and prepared to hire a carriage when suddenly a number of people looking like rickshaw pullers rushed forward, surrounding him. They started by arguing about the fare, then suddenly said sternly, you're a solo traveler with lots of luggage, do you know the rules around here? If you know what's good for you, you better hand over five dollars as a toll, or don't even think about moving an inch. And if you don't have cash, you can leave your clothes as collateral. Seeing that the gang was strong and violent, and unable to fight back, Tang decided to negotiate. In the end, he paid one dollar and two jiao as the toll. The gang then dispersed. After Tang got away, he reported the incident to the patrol officer. Three leaders were arrested: Han Changzhou, Zhao Jinshan, Yang Lianchenzi, all from Yancheng. They were then taken to the First District Main Office, waiting to be investigated by the district chief.

Deceptive Marriage of a Married Woman 199

Jiang A'er Was Noncommittal

The Guo Father and Son Re-Litigate

Jiang A'er, a woman from Wuzhen, Zhejiang, is 24 years old. A'er was furious because she was beaten and abused by her husband at home. On June 15 of the old calendar this year, she ran away alone to Shanghai and hid near Pengjiazhai in Pudong. Soon after, she met Jin Qiaojian, a woman from Huzhou who lived near the police station road. Qiaojian claimed that her husband's name was Qu Achun, who opened a recommendation shop, and ordered A'er to stay at her home to introduce people to be maids. A'er listened to the words and believed it was true, and immediately agreed. Long Cai, the son of Guo Wenzhi, a Haimen person living in Pengjiazhai, is now 25 years old and works as a boatman. Because his family is very poor, he has not yet married. Coincidentally, Qiaojian knew Guo well and knew that Guo had no wife, so she secretly discussed with her husband Achun to sell Jiang A'er to Guo as his wife to make a profit. After the plan was decided, they persuaded Guo, claiming that A'er was her sister, only 22 years old, and had not yet been betrothed to anyone, and she was willing to act as a matchmaker to make a good thing happen. Guo saw that A'er looked good and expressed satisfaction. Qiaojian then demanded a gift of 200 yuan, and later reduced it by 25 yuan, and settled at 175 yuan after both parties agreed. On the auspicious day of July 3 of the old calendar, A'er was sent to Guo's house to get married. A'er did not know the inside story, only knew that she was recommended by the shop owner to Guo's house to help work. Unexpectedly, when she arrived at the Guo's door, firecrackers were set off, and the house was full of incense and candles. At the same time, A'er was also pushed into the room and slightly decorated, and then she and Guo worshiped each other in front of the ceremony table. At this time, A'er was like falling into a fog, letting it be done. After spending the night with Guo, she asked about the details and told Guo that she was already a married woman and not Qiaojian's sister. Guo knew he had been fooled, and the next day he and his father Wenzhi prepared a statement requesting the local court to file the case, and lived with A'er in a perfunctory manner, just like a couple. Recently, the Guo father and son were afraid that A'er's original husband would find out after a long time, causing disputes, so they filed a statement with the local court accusing the Qiaojian couple of fraud and demanding the gift money. Yesterday, the court sent a document to the Pudong Third District Public Security Bureau to send the police to arrest the defendants Jin Qiaojian and her husband Qu Achun, and summoned the plaintiff Guo father and son and the person involved, Jiang A'er, to interrogate them one by one. The verdict was that they should be sent to the court for interrogation.

An Illegitimate Union 200

Should be Separated

No Need for Alimony

Nie Yongfu, also known as Xiao Dezi, lived in front of Meixielu. His wife, Tang, was called Aipangzi because she was short and fat. Xiao Dezi and Aipangzi were originally an illegitimate union. At first, they were very affectionate and got along very well for five or six years. In April of this year, Nie returned to his hometown of Yancheng, and Tang stayed in Shanghai and fell in love with Lin Dajuzi, who was a partner of Yang Chunshan, who lent money at high interest rates. In August, Nie returned to Shanghai and found out about it and beat Aipangzi, who then escaped. Nie then negotiated with Lin Dajuzi. Yang Chunshan was also present. At that time, there was a conflict, and as a result of jealousy, Nie and a friend were stabbed, and Yang Chunshan on Lin Dajuzi's side died, so Nie was detained. Fortunately, the court verified that Yang died of a chronic disease, so Nie was released on bail, but he had been in prison for a month. Unexpectedly, Aipangzi recently petitioned the civil court of the local court, accusing Nie of abuse, and used up the money left by her ex-husband, requesting a divorce and giving considerable alimony. The afternoon before yesterday, Judge Wang opened a court to hear the case. Nie filed a counterclaim, saying that after he returned to his hometown, his wife pawned two Zhigongni gowns, two gold rings, a gold bracelet, and 47 yuan in cash, all for the use of her lover, which could be investigated. The woman said that it was her pawned items before and should not be returned. It was immediately considered that the debate was over. Now it has been ruled that due to the illegitimate union, there is no contract and the relationship should be separated. Since it is an illegitimate union, there is no need for alimony and it is rejected. However, Tang should return the counterclaim filed by Nie.

Reuniting a Good Dream

Shan Hongqiu, 31 years old, from Yancheng, lived near Xiangyanqiao in Hongkou and worked as a worker. Yesterday, he personally filed a complaint with the Pudong Third District, saying that his wife, Zhou, was now hidden by his friend Li Sanguai near Lanidu in Pudong and occupied as his wife, requesting detention and investigation. As a result, the district chief allowed Shan to take his wife home and reunite a good dream.

Xu Xue, A Woman Having Affairs 202

Wang Mingda Has No Right to Interfere

Xu Xue, a woman from Danyang, is now 29 years old. Her husband went out to do business three years ago and his whereabouts are unknown. The family has nothing but empty walls and no constant property. Because of the difficult life at home, she brought her nine-year-old daughter Ai Di to Shanghai this spring to work in a yarn factory and stayed at the Zhao family, a fellow villager in Yangshupu. Zhao entrusted someone to recommend her to work in the coarse yarn room of the Yihe Yarn Factory. She is slightly beautiful, and although she is a middle-aged woman, she still has charm. Before long, she had an affair with Wang Mingda, a Zhenjiang person living nearby. Wang works as a tailor and is now 28 years old. Since the affair, she could not be blatant because she was staying at the Zhao family. So this summer, she moved out of the Zhao family on the pretext of returning home, and moved to the back building of a tailor shop on Lafayette Road in the French Concession with Wang to live together, just like a couple. She immediately led her daughter to a nearby cigarette factory to pack cigarettes. However, Wang's work was light in the summer and his monthly income was very small. He relied entirely on the wages earned by her to make up for the long-term expenses. She inevitably complained, so they often quarreled. She felt that Wang was difficult to grow old with, and she knew Cai Xiaoxiang, a street runner of the cigarette company, and built another love nest on the upper floor of the Fengtai small cigarette paper shop in Liangzhuqiaojia. She often went there with Cai for secret meetings. After a long time, Wang found out. At 8:00 PM the night before last, she was in the adulterous place with Cai, and Wang gathered thugs to catch the adulterers, and arrested her and Cai. After questioning by the head of the police station, Wang and she were not formal couples and had no right to interfere, and he refused to deal with it. The vinegar storm dispersed.

Simplified Rules for Permanent Propaganda Teams in District Branches 212

Revised and Promulgated by the Municipal Propaganda Department

The Propaganda Department of the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Committee, in order to increase the efficiency and agility of propaganda work, specially ordered all levels of Party committees in the city to organize permanent propaganda teams. The first expanded propaganda conference suggested revisions to the already promulgated simplified rules for permanent propaganda teams. The Municipal Propaganda Department has made these revisions and issued a notice to all levels of Party committees in the city, requiring all permanent propaganda teams to implement the new simplified rules. The new simplified rules are excerpted below:

Simplified Rules for Permanent Propaganda Teams in District Branches (Revised and Promulgated on November 2, 1930) Article 1: Each district branch shall organize a permanent propaganda team to increase the agility and efficiency of propaganda work. Article 2: The propaganda work of each district branch shall be primarily undertaken by the permanent propaganda team. Article 3: Members of the permanent propaganda team shall be selected from party members in each branch who have an interest in propaganda work and possess the necessary propaganda skills. Article 4: Members of the permanent propaganda team shall be elected by the party member congress of each district branch. Article 5: Each permanent propaganda team shall have at least five members. Article 6: Each permanent propaganda team shall have a captain, who shall be the propaganda committee member of the district branch. Article 7: Each permanent propaganda team shall have a secretary to assist the captain in handling team affairs. Article 8: The permanent propaganda team may convene team meetings at any time as needed. Article 9: The captain shall chair the team meetings, and the secretary shall record the minutes. Article 10: The team meetings may make resolutions, but they must be reported to the party member congress or the district branch executive committee at any time. Article 11: Within three days after each propaganda outing, the permanent propaganda team shall fill out a report form and submit it to the district propaganda committee and the municipal propaganda department. Article 12: The term of office for members of the permanent propaganda team shall be six months. After the term expires, a new team shall be organized. Members may be re-elected. Article 13: Each branch shall organize at least one permanent propaganda team. Article 14: These simplified rules shall be implemented after being promulgated by the Municipal Propaganda Department. Article 15: These simplified rules may be revised by the Municipal Propaganda Department at any time if they are not perfect.
