The Shanghai National Products Factory United Association received a telegram from the Ministry of Finance stating that the association had previously telegraphed regarding the confiscation and tax levy on products from the Dafeng Textile Factory by the Jiujiang Consumption Bureau and the Zhejiang Province Cloth Unified Tax Bureau. The ministry had instructed the Jiangxi Financial Commissioner and the Zhejiang Finance Bureau to investigate and stop the practice. The Jiangxi Financial Commissioner reported that they had complied and ordered the Jiujiang Consumption Tax Bureau that henceforth, products from the Dafeng Textile Factory, upon verification of the documents issued by the first customs office and confirmation that the documents and goods matched, should be exempted from taxes and released without difficulty or re-levying. The Ministry of Finance, Song, with seal, informed the association accordingly.

Second Meeting of Tenants in Tedenham Lee 216

Since the new landlord, Chengyu Company, announced the demolition of the houses in Tedenham Lee, Nanyang Bridge, in the French Concession, the tenants have been alarmed. They organized a tenants' association to negotiate with the landlord. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, all the tenants convened a second meeting at the Nanyang Bridge Business Association. All the tenants were present and elected Lin Zhengtang as chairman. He reported that the association had followed the previous resolution to send five representatives to demand that the landlord cancel the demolition plan. The association also sent a letter in the name of the tenants' association to request that the demolition be stopped. However, several rounds of negotiation were rejected. The landlord of Chengyu Company is Xing Dingcheng, a comprador of Sassoon & Co. The case of the houses in Qingyun Lane, Hongkou, remains unresolved. Now, he is forcing the tenants of Tedenham Lee to move out. How should we deal with this? Please discuss, he asked. The tenants expressed their opinions and unanimously advocated firm opposition. It was resolved to implement the following measures: (1) Gather all efforts to resist to the death. No matter what, we will never move. (2) The tenants' association will issue a declaration detailing the age of the houses and the illegal oppression and forced eviction by the landlord, and inform all citizens of the city to rise up and overthrow the housing barons. (3) Make slogans and distribute them to each tenant to post to show the spirit of unity. (4) Submit petitions to the Chinese and French authorities requesting measures to stop the demolition. (5) Raise funds to hire lawyers to protect our rights according to the law. The meeting adjourned.

Meeting Minutes of Yongkang Lane Tenants 217

The Yongkang Lane area on North Sichuan Road has a total of fifty buildings. In the past, the Yongkang Company leased land to build houses for a term of twenty years. There are only three years left until the lease expires. Now, the company has sold these houses to Wanfu Company and plans to demolish them immediately, ordering all tenants to move out. The tenants are greatly alarmed because the land lease for these houses will expire soon and there is no need to demolish them. It has also been found that the company will take back the houses, make some repairs, and increase the rent from 16 yuan per month to 35 yuan. Therefore, they jointly hired a lawyer and filed a lawsuit with the local court to prevent the relocation. The case has been heard several times without a resolution, and a settlement has been ordered. Yesterday, the Yongkang Lane Tenants' Association held a meeting to discuss the situation. Chairman Zheng Guogan reported on the settlement situation in court by Judge Zhao. Then, Executive Committee member Ouyang Hengyi spoke up, saying that a Mr. Zhou had come to see him the other day, claiming to be a representative of the landlord, and offered 1,400 yuan to have the tenants move out, which the Executive Committee member rejected. The crowd discussed it for a long time before adjourning the meeting.

Shaoxing Native Place Association Elects President and Vice Presidents 218

The Shaoxing Seven Counties Native Place Association in Shanghai held a meeting of the new board of directors and a board of directors meeting of the school yesterday at the association's premises at No. 26 Algin Road. The minutes are recorded separately below:

School Board of Directors Meeting: Since the First School affiliated with the association was reorganized this summer and Tang Liqing was hired as principal, there has been much progress in school affairs. Yesterday was the date of the fourth regular meeting of the school's board of directors. The meeting was convened at the association's premises. Eight directors, including Shou Xiaotian, attended, and the school principal, Tang Liqing, attended as an observer. The meeting began with formalities and a report by Principal Tang, followed by a discussion of: (1) The proposal to expand the school's enrollment. It was resolved to expand the enrollment to 300 students from the next semester and convert the school into a complete elementary school. (2) The proposal to add free student places. It was resolved to change the ratio to one free student place for every ten students. (3) Principal Tang Liqing requested to add teaching materials. It was resolved to approve 76 yuan according to the list. (Remaining items omitted.) The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

New Term Meeting: The association held a general meeting of members on the 26th of last month, resulting in the election of eighty new directors. The first meeting of the directors was convened yesterday, with more than fifty directors, including Hu Xisheng and Shou Xiaotian, attending. Hu Xisheng was elected as chairman. The meeting began with formalities, followed by reports and discussions. Wang 籁 was elected as president, and Wang Yansong and Hu Xisheng were elected as vice presidents. Shou Xiaotian and Tang Deshi, among others, were elected as directors.

News from Various Labor Unions 219

The Shanghai Merchants Steam Navigation Company No. 5 Wharf Workers' Union held its seventh regular meeting of the board of directors yesterday. Resolutions: (1) The Huazhan branch's executive committee submitted a request to oppose the leasing of Huazhan Wharf, along with a written opinion. It was resolved to forward the letter to the general bureau to express their opinion. (2) The Zhongzhan branch's executive committee submitted a request to oppose the leasing of Huazhan Wharf. It was resolved to handle it together with the previous case. (3) The Beizhan branch's executive committee submitted a request for unemployment benefits for five members of the wharf crew. It was resolved that since the five had resigned voluntarily, unemployment benefits should not be discussed. (4) The Huazhan branch's executive committee reported that a vacancy had been created due to the death of a worker, and proposed that member trainee Ma Laigeng be promoted. It was resolved to forward the request to the general bureau for approval. (5) The Huazhan branch's executive committee submitted a letter from Wang Xingbi, who had been expelled from the union, requesting to be reinstated. It was resolved to submit it to the organization department for review and then decide. (6) The entertainment committee requested funding to purchase various board games. It was resolved to allocate twelve yuan from the general affairs department. (7) Huang Jin要求 requested one month's retirement pay. It was resolved to approve it. (8) Zhou Pingshu 德华 submitted a letter to defend himself and request reinstatement. It was resolved to convene a meeting of group leaders at 10:00 AM on November 5 to discuss it. No temporary motions.

The China General Edison Company Labor Union held its second joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees the other day. Chairman Zhu Hanhe led the meeting with formalities. (A) Report Items (Omitted) (B) Discussion Items (1) Members who have not paid their union dues and are past the deadline. It was resolved that their membership would be suspended for three months from the final deadline, and the names of the suspended members would be published in detail in the union's monthly magazine. (2) The Beijing Opera group sent a letter requesting a representative to attend the opening of the group's meeting. It was resolved to comply. (3) Comrade Wu Xiangming resigned from all union positions for no reason to the general affairs department. It was resolved that the joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees would send a letter asking for a detailed reason for the resignation. (4) Executive Committee member Li Yu passed away, and the number of executive committee members is insufficient, so it should be filled. It was resolved that alternate member Jia Renjie would fill the position. (5) Sick leave for workers should be handled in accordance with the union's agreement with the company. It was resolved that the union would send another letter to handle it. (6) When a worker resigns, they should be informed of their rights and the union dues they should pay. It was resolved that the union rights a worker is entitled to should be based on the last day the company paid their retirement salary, and that dues should be paid up to that date. (7) Workers' welfare fund. It was resolved to collect one cent more of each worker's salary starting December 1. (8) Regarding the membership of mechanical apprentices and train attendants in the future. It was resolved that mechanical apprentices can only join the union after working for one year from the date of registration, and train attendants can only join the union after becoming regular workers from the date of registration. (9) The date of the memorial service for deceased worker Comrade Li Yu. It was resolved that it would be held on November 24 (Monday). (Remaining items omitted).

The British Municipal Council Electricity Department Labor Union held a regular meeting yesterday. Chairman Chen Gengsheng resolved the following cases: (1) Member Xie Jin first worked poorly and was dismissed by the factory. Zhuyin first came to the union to request protection. It was resolved that the member was in arrears of union fees for more than ten months, so the union could not protect him. (2) Wang Xigui proposed that there have recently been unscrupulous elements spreading rumors and defaming the union in the factory. How should it be handled? It was resolved that if anyone damages the union's reputation again and is confirmed by investigation, they will be warned for the first offense and expelled for the second offense. (3) Secret. (4) Member Su Akang passed away due to illness. The company gave him 735 yuan and 60 cents in retirement and funeral expenses. Should the union express its gratitude? It was resolved to pass it.

The Candle Industry Whole Committee convened an emergency meeting of members yesterday, with 70 people attending. Chairman Chen Zenghao, the agenda was as follows: (1) The former standing committee requested a subsidy from the union. By public vote, it was denied. (2) Salary increase issues. (1) After students graduate, their wages will increase by two yuan per year. (2) Workers' wages will be increased by 30%, with a minimum increase of one yuan. Round-trip travel expenses will be increased by four yuan. Summer overtime will be paid as usual. By public vote, it was resolved to send a letter to the Candle Industry Workers' Union to request it from the management.

Weather Report 220

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the sky was overcast and cold, with rain or snow on the Shandong coast. There were strong northwesterly winds over the Bohai Sea. There were northerly to northeasterly winds over the Yellow Sea and East China Sea. In addition, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this port was 55.9 degrees and the lowest was 43.5 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 69.2 degrees and the lowest was 38.4 degrees.

Special Article

A Retrospective and Prospective View of the Chinese Children's Welfare Association (Continued) Wu Weide 221

In the area of social education, our association, in order to promote child welfare work, popularize child welfare knowledge, and facilitate the child welfare movement, held a grand child welfare movement conference for four days starting from the 7th of December in the 18th year of the Republic, at the Martyr's Hall of the Shanghai YMCA. The aim was to arouse social sympathy and promote the success of child welfare undertakings. A total of 86 cooperating organizations, 530 cooperating personnel, and over 40,000 guests attended the conference, distributing over 70,000 copies of publications. Exhibits came from twelve provinces and regions within the country. Children from neighboring countries such as Japan, Russia, France, England, and the United States also enthusiastically participated in the performances, truly making it an unprecedented grand event. Furthermore, in the Zhabei area of Shanghai, there are many poor households. Due to the public's lack of hygiene knowledge, diseases are rampant, especially with the most infant deaths. Therefore, in June of this year, our association specifically held a hygiene movement conference for two days starting from the 18th at the address of our association's Child Welfare Education and Rearing Institute, with the aim of arousing the awareness of local residents and promoting fundamental remedies. A total of 37 cooperating organizations participated, with 88 people receiving physical examinations, 200 people receiving extended medical treatment and model bathing, 1,166 people receiving cholera vaccinations, over 1,000 primary school students participating in the parade, over 10,000 people visiting the hygiene exhibition, and over 40,000 people watching the hygiene education film. It can also be said to be a grand event.

China's child welfare undertakings originated very early. During the Southern Song Dynasty, the government established the Bureau of Child Welfare. So-called infant asylums, orphanages, relief homes for orphans, and homes for poor children can be found in any large city. Although the number is still insufficient, because they are each independently managed and do not communicate with each other, the spirit is extremely loose and isolated. It is difficult to expect the effect of mutual learning, observation, and unified progress. Our association is the only organization in China that coordinates the welfare of all children. Naturally, we should find ways to remedy and gradually improve the situation, and we believe that this is our inescapable and undeniable duty. Therefore, we are now working to connect child welfare organizations across the country, starting with investigating the current situation, hoping to unite these scattered and unconnected child welfare organizations into a whole, systematic large child welfare body. Then, we will concentrate the strength of this large child welfare body to promote the happiness of Chinese children and realize the ideals of the child welfare movement. This certainly cannot be regarded as anything less than a great work. In addition, we are eagerly seeking comrades to establish child welfare branches throughout the country, hoping to build our China into a China centered on the happiness of children. What is our goal? According to the International Child Welfare Association of the League of Nations, it has established several principles regarding the protection of children's rights, and notified governments of all countries to follow them uniformly. What are the principles of the so-called Geneva Declaration of the Rights of the Child? The contents of these principles are listed below: First, children should enjoy all kinds of material and spiritual rights in order to fully achieve their proper development. Second, the principle of treating children is to feed them when they are hungry, care for them when they are sick, influence them when they are misled, uplift them when they are lagging behind, and provide relief when they are destitute. Third, save children first when encountering danger. Fourth, children should have opportunities to earn a living and should receive appropriate protection. Fifth, we should teach children to realize from an early age that they have a responsibility to serve society to the best of their ability. Now that we know what the standards of children's rights are, let us compare them with the living conditions of Chinese children and see how they compare. Have Chinese children enjoyed the rights they should enjoy?

The target of the Chinese Child Welfare Association is 120 million children, a number equal to the entire population of the United States. Our country's infant mortality rate is the highest in the world, except for India. This is completely a waste. In New Zealand, the infant mortality rate is less than 40 per thousand, while in our country, even according to the lowest estimate, out of every thousand children, 250 die before their first birthday. Every year, our country loses about 10 million young citizens. If children could have their safety planned for and relief implemented, how could it be like this? According to the Ministry of Education's survey, our country has a total of 43 million school-age children, but in reality, only 6.5 million of them enjoy the right to attend school. The remaining more than 80% of children are completely out of school, wasting their golden years. In several provinces in the Northwest, there are famines, and about 5,000 people die of cold and hunger every day. What could be more tragic than this? Nationwide, there are now no fewer than 200,000 children who have fallen into the status of slaves and spend their days living an inhuman life. In addition, countless children with sallow faces and emaciated bodies are begging on the streets. Alas, pity these innocents who are born into misfortune, and have compassion on these children, how can we bear it? All those who embrace humanitarianism, seeing this painful phenomenon, how can they not shed tears of sympathy? How can we provide relief to them and enable them to enjoy the opportunity for proper development? That is naturally the responsibility of us elders. How can we unite comrades and concentrate the strength of organizations to eradicate evil forces and seek happiness for them? That is naturally the step we elders should take. This is the mission of the Chinese Child Welfare Association. (To be continued)

Market News 222

The Shilu Daxin Silk and Satin Bureau announced that since its opening, due to its excellent selection of goods and low prices, business has been exceptionally prosperous. The weather has suddenly turned cold in recent days, and people from all walks of life need to make winter clothes. This is precisely the time when the bureau is holding its autumn sale, so customers are extremely crowded. In particular, domestically produced silk and satin such as figured and plain wool crepe, electric motor crepe, brocade ground crepe, red cloud crepe, various colors of Hangzhou satin, and Qilin crepe flower line printed soft satin are most appreciated by ladies and gentlemen from all walks of life. Daily sales exceed ten thousand yuan. The bureau's autumn sale period has only seven days left. Ladies and gentlemen from all walks of life should not miss this good opportunity, and so on.

The Huaxin Company in Nanjing Road Central City announced that since the company held its third anniversary gift certificate giveaway, the prosperity of its business has been truly astonishing. In view of this, the company has specially continued to sacrifice and give away gift certificates for seven days and shipped in thick wool coats from Europe and the United States, each at a special price of twelve yuan. Various leather bags, silk woven clothing edges, and various clothing materials are the most fashionable goods. And beautiful coats, capes, Chinese and Western art leather shoes, etc., are all sold at particularly low prices, and so on.

The Zhongxi Pharmacy on Fourth Malu announced that the sixteen-year-old girl Xuehua, managed by this pharmacy, has seen a sharp increase in sales due to her clean color, fragrant aroma, luxurious decoration, and reasonable pricing. Daily retail and wholesale to various ports are no less than thousands of dozens, with a large trend of supply falling short of demand, and so on.

The Langji Business Engineering Company announced that this company specializes in planning and packaging tap water, artesian wells, sanitary appliances, heating and refrigeration, ice plants, electric lights and motors, and various construction projects. It holds Shanghai Municipal Government Water Pipe Business License No. 1, Well Drilling Project License No. 1, and Electrical Material Business License No. 120. It has completed no fewer than hundreds of bank, residential, and factory projects. It is generally praised for its accurate engineering and outstanding reputation. Now, in order to expand its business, it has specially moved to No. 141 Tiantong Road, to the Tianxing six-story Western-style building on the corner of Zhapu Road for its office. The equipment there was also planned and packaged by this company. If all sectors favor us, regardless of the size of the project, all are welcome. Please move to the new office to contact us. Telephone number is 40791, and so on.
